# **II. Software Requirement Specification** {#ii.-software-requirement-specification}

## **1\. Overall Requirements** {#1.-overall-requirements}

### **1.1 Context Diagram** {#1.1-context-diagram}

The Smart Quiz Platform (SQP) is an open online learning and assessment platform where anyone can discover, create, share, study, and evaluate learning content. Guests can access public study sets and flashcards, while registered users can use the same account as either Learner or Teacher and switch roles when needed.

Learners can join classes, use AI features with Premium access, study with flashcards, take quizzes, review wrong answers, and track progress. Teachers can also create study sets and questions, while additionally managing classes, assigning study sets, configuring exams, viewing analytics, and exporting reports. The platform supports Premium upgrades through a Payment Gateway, AI features through Gemini API, authentication through Supabase, notifications through Email Service, and system management by Admins.

![][image2]

_Diagram 1: Context diagram of Smart Quiz Platform (SQP)_

### **1.3 User Requirements** {#1.3-user-requirements}

#### **_1.3.1 Actors_**

| \#  | Actor                   | Description                                                                                                                                            |
| --- | :---------------------- | :----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| 1   | Guest                   | An unregistered user who accesses the platform to view general information or try out flashcards.                                                      |
| 2   | Learner                 | A learner who interacts with study sets, enters classes, participates in exams, and views mistakes.                                                    |
| 3   | Teacher                 | An educator who creates classes online, manages question banks, create study sets, configures exam sessions, and exports scoreboards.                  |
| 4   | Admin                   | A high-level administrator responsible for managing user accounts, configuring role permissions, and monitoring the overall stability of the platform. |
| 5   | Supabase Authentication | An external system that manages user login, session management, and account security.                                                                  |
| 6   | Email Service           | An external system used to send automated exam reminders, test results, and updates from teachers to learners.                                         |
| 7   | Payment Gateway         | An external payment gateway that processes transactions for Premium upgrades or paying service fees.                                                   |
| 8   | Gemini API              | An external artificial intelligence service used to generate questions, explain answers, and analyze learning content                                  |

_Table 1: Table of Actors in Smart Quiz Platform_

#### **_1.3.2 Use Cases (UC)_**

| ID    | Use Case                         | Actor                   | Feature                  | Use Case Description                                                                                                                                                                           |
| :---- | :------------------------------- | :---------------------- | :----------------------- | :--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| UC-01 | View landing page                | Guest, Learner, Teacher | Public Access            | Guest views the landing page of the platform.                                                                                                                                                  |
| UC-02 | Search public study sets         | Guest, Learner          | Public Access            | Guest, Learner searches public study sets by keyword.                                                                                                                                          |
| UC-03 | Search public user accounts      | Guest, Learner          | Public Access            | Guest, Learner searches public user accounts by keyword.                                                                                                                                       |
| UC-04 | View public study set detail     | Guest, Learner          | Public Access            | Guest, Learner views details of a public study set, including title, description, subject, owner information, and learning content.                                                     |
| UC-05 | Study flashcards                 | Guest, Learner          | Study Set Learning       | Guest, Learner studies a study set using flashcard mode.                                                                                                                                       |
| UC-06 | View premium plans               | Guest, Learner, Teacher | Payment & Subscription   | Guest, Learner, or Teacher views available Premium plans and their benefits.                                                                                                                   |
| UC-07 | Register account                 | Guest                   | Authentication           | Guest creates a new account on the platform.                                                                                                                                                   |
| UC-08 | Log in with account              | Guest                   | Authentication           | Guest logs in to the platform using a registered account and valid credentials.                                                                                                                |
| UC-09 | Log in with Google               | Guest                   | Authentication           | Guest logs in to the platform using a Google account. The system authenticates the user through Google OAuth and creates or retrieves the corresponding platform account.                      |
| UC-10 | Forgot password                  | Guest                   | Authentication           | Guest requests and completes a password reset when they forget their password.                                                                                                                 |
| UC-11 | Log out account                  | Learner, Teacher, Admin | Authentication           | User logs out from the current session.                                                                                                                                                        |
| UC-12 | View personal profile            | Learner, Teacher, Admin | Profile Management       | User views their personal profile information.                                                                                                                                                 |
| UC-13 | Edit personal profile            | Learner, Teacher, Admin | Profile Management       | User updates allowed personal profile information.                                                                                                                                             |
| UC-14 | Change password                  | Learner, Teacher, Admin | Profile Management       | User changes their account password.                                                                                                                                                           |
| UC-15 | Switch account role              | Learner, Teacher        | Profile Management       | User switches their active role between Learner and Teacher. After switching, the system redirects the user to the corresponding dashboard and applies permissions based on the selected role. |
| UC-16 | Upgrade to Premium               | Learner, Teacher        | Payment & Subscription   | Learner or Teacher selects a Premium plan, completes payment, and receives Premium access after the payment is successful.                                                                     |
| UC-17 | View joined classes              | Learner                 | Class Management         | Learner views the list of classes they have joined.                                                                                                                                            |
| UC-18 | Join class                       | Learner                 | Class Management         | Learner joins a class using a valid class code or invitation link.                                                                                                                             |
| UC-19 | View accessible study sets       | Learner, Teacher        | Study Set Learning       | Learner views public or assigned study sets. Teacher views public, owned, or authorized study sets.                                                                                            |
| UC-20 | Take study set quiz              | Learner                 | Study Set Learning       | Learner takes a quiz generated from a study set.                                                                                                                                               |
| UC-21 | Review wrong answers             | Learner                 | Study Set Learning       | Learner views and redoes the list of questions they answered incorrectly after completing quiz mode.                                                                                           |
| UC-22 | Request AI answer explanation    | Learner                 | Study Set Learning       | Learner requests an AI-generated explanation for a question and answer if they have active Premium access .                                                                                    |
| UC-23 | View personal learning progress  | Learner                 | Analytics & Reports      | Learner views personal learning progress, including practiced questions, accuracy rate, repeated mistakes, and weak subjects.                                                                    |
| UC-24 | View available exams             | Learner                 | Exam Session Management  | Learner views exam sessions available to them.                                                                                                                                                 |
| UC-25 | View available exam information  | Learner                 | Exam Session Management  | Learner views exam information such as exam time, duration, number of attempts, and result visibility rule.                                                                                    |
| UC-26 | Take exam                        | Learner                 | Exam Session Management  | Learner takes an exam by starting the attempt, answering exam questions and submitting the exam.                                                                                               |
| UC-27 | View exam result                 | Learner                 | Exam Session Management  | Learner views exam result if the teacher allows result visibility.                                                                                                                             |
| UC-28 | View created classes             | Teacher                 | Class Management         | Teacher views the list of classes they created or are assigned to.                                                                                                                             |
| UC-29 | Create class                     | Teacher                 | Class Management         | Teacher creates a class. The system automatically generates a class code and invitation link.                                                                                                  |
| UC-30 | View class member list           | Teacher                 | Class Management         | Teacher views the list of learners in a class.                                                                                                                                                 |
| UC-31 | Approve class join request       | Teacher                 | Class Management         | Teacher approves a learner request to join the class.                                                                                                                                          |
| UC-32 | Remove learner from class        | Teacher                 | Class Management         | Teacher removes a learner from a class.                                                                                                                                                        |
| UC-33 | View question banks              | Teacher                 | Question Bank Repository | Teacher views the reusable question banks they created or are authorized to access for repeated study set or exam creation.                                                                    |
| UC-34 | Create question bank             | Teacher                 | Question Bank Repository | Teacher creates a new question bank as a reusable repository for questions that can be selected for study sets or exam sessions.                                                               |
| UC-35 | Update question bank information | Teacher                 | Question Bank Repository | Teacher updates question bank title, description, subject, visibility, or repository configuration.                                                                                     |
| UC-36 | Delete question bank             | Teacher                 | Question Bank Repository | Teacher deletes, archives, or hides a question bank that is no longer needed, subject to integrity rules for exams and historical records.                                                     |
| UC-37 | Add question manually            | Teacher                 | Question Management      | Teacher manually adds questions to owned or authorized Study Sets and Question Banks.                                                                                                          |
| UC-38 | Import questions from Excel      | Teacher                 | Question Management      | Teacher imports questions by Excel into authorized Study Sets or Question Banks.                                                                                                               |
| UC-39 | View question import errors      | Teacher                 | Question Management      | Teacher views row-level validation errors for imported questions before saving valid rows.                                                                                                     |
| UC-40 | Preview questions before saving  | Teacher                 | Question Management      | Teacher previews manually entered, imported, copied, or AI-generated questions before saving them into an authorized question container.                                                       |
| UC-41 | Update question                  | Teacher                 | Question Management      | Teacher updates question content, answer options, correct answer, score, explanation, tags, or chapter inside an authorized question container.            |
| UC-42 | Delete question                  | Teacher                 | Question Management      | Teacher deletes, removes, hides, or archives a question from an authorized question container, subject to historical learning, exam, and reporting integrity rules.                            |
| UC-43 | Generate questions from material | Teacher                 | Question Management      | Teacher generates questions from uploaded learning material using AI and saves those questions to Study Sets or Question Banks if they have active Premium access .                            |
| UC-44 | Create study set                 | Teacher                 | Study Set Management     | Teacher creates a Study Set, then adds questions. Teachers may also choose questions from a Question Bank into the Study Set.                                                                  |
| UC-45 | Assign study set to class        | Teacher                 | Study Set Management     | Teacher assigns a study set to a class.                                                                                                                                                        |
| UC-46 | Create exam session              | Teacher                 | Exam Session Management  | Teacher creates an official exam session for a class using selected questions or an authorized question bank.                                                                                  |
| UC-47 | Configure exam settings          | Teacher                 | Exam Session Management  | Teacher configures exam time, allowed attempts, question and answer randomization, and result visibility.                                                                                      |
| UC-48 | View own exam information        | Teacher                 | Exam Session Management  | Teacher views configured exam information, including selected class, questions, exam time, attempt limit, randomization, and result visibility.                                                |
| UC-49 | View learning analytics          | Teacher                 | Analytics & Report       | Teacher views learning, exam, learner, question, and class performance analytics.                                                                                                              |
| UC-50 | Export report                    | Teacher                 | Analytics & Report       | Teacher exports scoreboards or reports to Excel, PDF, or CSV.                                                                                                                                  |
| UC-51 | View user list                   | Admin                   | System Admin             | Admin views the list of users in the system.                                                                                                                                                   |
| UC-52 | Update user account status       | Admin                   | System Admin             | Admin updates user account status such as active, suspended, or banned.                                                                                                                        |
| UC-53 | Hide public learning resource    | Admin                   | System Admin             | Admin hides inappropriate or invalid public learning resources such as public study sets or other public learning content.                                                                     |
| UC-54 | View system status               | Admin                   | System Admin             | Admin views the operational status of the platform.                                                                                                                                            |
