### **1.5 Entity Relationship Diagram** {#1.5-entity-relationship-diagram}

![][image14]

_Diagram 13: Entity Relationship Diagram for Smart Quiz Platform_

**Entities Description**

| \#  | Entity           | Description                                                                                                                                                                   |
| :-- | :--------------- | :---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| 1   | Learner          | A student or learner who joins classes, creates and manages owned study sets, practices study sets, takes exams, submits answers, and uses learning features in the platform. |
| 2   | Teacher          | An educator who creates and manages classes, question banks, study sets, exams, and reports.                                                                                  |
| 3   | Class            | An online learning class created by a teacher where learners can join, receive study sets, and participate in exams.                                                          |
| 4   | Join Request     | A request submitted by a learner to join a class, which can be reviewed or approved by a teacher.                                                                             |
| 5   | Question Bank    | A collection of questions created or managed by a teacher for study, practice, or exam purposes.                                                                              |
| 6   | Question         | A learning or assessment item that belongs to a question bank and can be used in study sets, practice sessions, or exams.                                                     |
| 7   | Answer Option    | A possible answer choice for a question.                                                                                                                                      |
| 8   | Study Set        | A group of selected questions used by learners for flashcard study or quiz practice.                                                                                          |
| 9   | Practice Session | A learning session where a learner practices a study set and answers questions outside of an official exam.                                                                   |
| 10  | Learner Answer   | The answer submitted by a learner during a practice session or exam attempt.                                                                                                  |
| 11  | Exam             | An official assessment created by a teacher and assigned to a class.                                                                                                          |
| 12  | Exam Attempt     | A learner’s attempt to take an exam, including submitted answers, completion status, score, and result information.                                                           |
| 13  | Report           | A report or scoreboard generated from class, exam, learner performance, or learning analytics data.                                                                           |
| 14  | Payment          | A payment transaction made by a learner or teacher for a premium plan.                                                                                                        |
| 15  | Premium Plan     | A paid service plan that provides learners or teachers with access to premium features.                                                                                       |
| 16  | AI Interaction   | An interaction between a learner or teacher and the AI service, such as requesting answer explanations or generating questions.                                               |

_Table 5: Table of entity relationship in Smart Quiz Platform_

## **2\. Use Case Specifications** {#2.-use-case-specifications}

### **2.1 Public Access & Discovery** {#2.1-public-access-&-discovery}

#### **_2.1.1 View landing page_** {#2.1.1-view-landing-page}

| ID and Name:       | UC-01 View landing page                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Vương Trung Quốc                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               | Date Created:     | 22/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Guest, Learner, Teacher                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        | Secondary Actors: | None      |
| Description:       | As a Guest, Learner, or Teacher, I want to view the platform landing page so that I can understand SQP’s main features, explore public learning resources, and decide whether to register, log in, or continue using the platform.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The user enters the platform URL in a web browser or clicks a link directing to the landing page.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The system is online and accessible over the network. PRE-2. The user has an active internet connection and a compatible web browser.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The system successfully renders the landing page for the user. POST-2. The system allows the user to browse public content or navigate to authentication pages. POST-3. If the user is already authenticated, the system displays navigation options according to the user’s active role.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-01.0 View Landing Page** 1\. The user navigates to the platform’s base URL. 2\. The system receives the request and checks whether the user has an active session. 3\. The system renders the landing page, displaying the welcome banner, platform introduction, public learning resources, and navigation options. 4\. If the user is unauthenticated, the system displays Login and Register options. 5\. If the user is authenticated, the system displays role-based navigation options. 6\. The user browses the landing page content and may interact with public elements.        |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-01.1 Authenticated User Views Landing Page** 1\. At step 2 of the Normal Flow, the system identifies an active session. 2\. The system identifies the user’s active role. 3\. The system renders the landing page with personalized navigation options. 4\. The user browses the landing page. **UC-01.2 No Public Resources Available** 1\. At step 3 of the Normal Flow, the system finds no public study sets or flashcards matching public visibility criteria. 2\. The system renders the landing page without public resource items and displays MSG45. 3\. The use case continues. |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-01.0.E1 Server Error or Maintenance** 1\. At any step, the system encounters an internal error or is down for maintenance. 2\. The system displays MSG13 or a maintenance notification. 3\. The use case ends.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | Very High. This is the entry point for almost all new visitors and returning users.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-01                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |           |
| Other Information: | The landing page serves as the primary marketing and discovery page. Performance and loading speed are critical for this use case.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The system caching mechanism is optimized to handle high volumes of Guest traffic without requiring heavy database queries for every visit.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |           |

####

#### **_2.1.2 Search public study sets_** {#2.1.2-search-public-study-sets}

| ID and Name:       | UC-02 Search public study sets                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Vương Trung Quốc                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      | Date Created:     | 22/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Guest, Learner                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        | Secondary Actors: |           |
| Description:       | As a Guest or Learner, I want to search public study sets by keyword so that I can find relevant learning materials quickly.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The user enters a keyword into the search bar and submits the search request.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The User (Guest or authenticated Learner) has accessed the platform. PRE-2. The search functionality is active and accessible.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The system successfully retrieves and displays a list of public study sets matching the search criteria.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-2.0 Search Public Study Sets** 1\. The user navigates to the search bar. 2\. The user enters a search keyword related to a study set's title, subject, or description. 3\. The system queries the database for study sets that match the keyword, ensuring their visibility status is "Public" and they have not been hidden by an Admin. 4\. The system renders and displays the search results, showing basic details. 5\. The user views the search results.                                                                                                    |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-2.1 Apply Search Filters** 1\. The user enters a search keyword and selects additional filters. 2\. The system queries the database using both the keyword and the applied filters. 3\. The system displays the refined list of matching public study sets. 4\. The user views the filtered results. **UC-2.2. No results found** 1\. The system queries the database but finds no public study sets matching the keyword (or all matching sets are private). 2\. The system displays a message (MSG45) and suggests the user try different or broader keywords. |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-2.0. E1 Invalid search input** 1\. The user submits an empty search query or a query containing only unsupported special characters. 2\. The system displays the message (MSG03) and asks the user to enter a valid search keyword. 3\. The use case ends.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | High. This is a primary discovery tool used frequently by both Guests exploring the platform and Learners looking for specific materials.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-01, BR-02, BR-03                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |
| Other Information: | \- Search results should ideally be paginated. \- The search algorithm may prioritize exact matches or popular study sets to improve the user experience.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | \- The system utilizes an efficient indexing or search mechanism capable of handling text-based queries rapidly. \- The database correctly maintains the visibility state of all study sets.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |           |

####

#### **_2.1.3 Search public user accounts_** {#2.1.3-search-public-user-accounts}

| ID and Name:       | UC-03 Search public user accounts                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Vương Trung Quốc                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             | Date Created:     | 23/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Guest, Learner                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               | Secondary Actors: |           |
| Description:       | As a Guest or Learner, I want to search public user accounts so that I can discover public profiles and learning resources shared by other users.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The user enters a keyword into the search bar and submits the search request.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The user has accessed the platform. PRE-2. The search functionality is active and functioning correctly.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The system successfully retrieves and displays a list of active public user accounts matching the search criteria. POST-2. The system does not expose any private user information in the search results.                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-3.0 Search Public User Accounts** 1\. The user navigates to the user search function. 2\. The user enters a search keyword and initiates the search. 3\. The system finds active user accounts matching the keyword, ensuring only public profile data is retrieved. 4\. The system renders the search results, displaying basic public information for each matching account. 5\. The user reviews the search results. |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-3.1 Access User Profile** 1\. While reviewing the search results, the user clicks on a specific user account. 2\. The system redirects the user to the public profile page of the selected user. **UC-3.2. No users found** 1\. The system queries the database but finds no users matching the keyword. 2\. The system displays a message (MSG45) and suggests the user try something different.                       |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-3.0. E1 Invalid search input** 1\. The user submits an empty query or a query with invalid special characters. 2\. The system ignores the request or displays a validation error (MSG03) prompting for a valid keyword. 3\. The use case ends.                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |           |
| Priority:          | Medium                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | Medium. Used when users want to find specific classmates, instructors, or content creators on the platform.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-01, BR-03                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |           |
| Other Information: | \- To optimize database performance, the search query should be indexed on frequently searched fields like name and username. \- Pagination or infinite scrolling should be implemented to handle search queries that return a large number of users.                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The system clearly differentiates between public profile data and private account data, ensuring strict data privacy compliance during the search process.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |

####

#### **_2.1.4 View public study set detail_** {#2.1.4-view-public-study-set-detail}

| ID and Name:       | UC-04 View public study set detail                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Vương Trung Quốc                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | Date Created:     | 23/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Guest, Learner                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    | Secondary Actors: |           |
| Description:       | As a Guest or Learner, I want to view the details of a public study set so that I can review its title, description, subject, and learning content before studying it.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The user clicks on a public study set link from the homepage, search results, or accesses it via a direct URL.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The selected study set exists in the system. PRE-2. The selected study set's visibility is set to Public and it has not been hidden by an Admin.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The system successfully displays the study set details and its associated learning content. POST-2. The system provides access buttons to available public study modes.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-4.0 View Public Study Set Detail** 1\. The user selects a specific public study set to view. 2\. The system verifies the visibility status and accessibility of the requested study set. 3\. The system retrieves the study set details and the complete list of content. 4\. The system renders the study set detail page, displaying all retrieved information. 5\. The user views the study set and scrolls through the learning content. |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-4.1 Change Content Display Format** 1\. While viewing the study set details, the user clicks the option to change the layout (e.g., from List view to Grid view). 2\. The system rearranges and displays the learning content according to the selected layout.                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-4.0. E1 Study set is private or hidden** 1\. The system detects that the requested study set is private or has been hidden by an Admin. 2\. The system blocks access and displays an error message (MSG34). 3\. The use case ends.                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | High. Viewing study material details is a core activity performed frequently by users exploring the platform.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-01, BR-02, BR-03, BR-04                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |           |
| Other Information: | \- Public study set detail pages should be optimized to allow external search engines to index the learning content and attract new Guests to the platform. \- The UI should clearly indicate if the user needs to log in to access specific restricted modes related to the study set.                                                                                                                                                           |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The system's access control mechanism is robust enough to strictly verify resource visibility (Public vs. Private) before rendering the page, ensuring private data is never leaked via direct URL access.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |           |

####

### **2.2 Authentication & Profile** {#2.2-authentication-&-profile}

#### **_2.2.1 Register account_** {#2.2.1-register-account}

| ID and Name:       | UC-07 Register account                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |                         |
| :----------------- | :--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :---------------------- |
| Created By:        | Phạm Minh Hải                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | Date Created:     | 20/5/2026               |
| Primary Actor:     | Guest                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          | Secondary Actors: | Supabase Authentication |
| Description:       | As a Guest, I want to register a new account so that I can access authenticated learning, class, exam, and profile features.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |                         |
| Trigger:           | The guest clicks the "Register" or "Sign Up" button on the landing page or login view.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |                         |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The user is not currently authenticated or logged into the system. PRE-2. The registration interface is online, active, and accessible.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |                         |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The system stores the new user account and credential relationship securely in the database. POST-2. The system updates the login status to authenticate in the user interface. POST-3. The user's personalized default settings and profile configurations are initialized accordingly.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |                         |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-07.0 Register Account** 1\. The Guest opens the Registration page. 2\. The system displays the registration form. 3\. The Guest enters required fields such as full name, username, email, password, and confirm password. 4\. The Guest submits the form. 5\. The system validates required fields, email uniqueness, input format, and password confirmation. 6\. The system creates the account through Supabase Authentication and local profile records. 7\. The system displays MSG01 and redirects the user according to onboarding rules.                                         |                   |                         |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-07.1 Cancel Registration** 1\. The Guest clicks Cancel before submission. 2\. The system discards unsaved registration data. 3\. The system returns the Guest to the previous public page.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |                         |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-7.0. E1 Email already exists** 1\. The system displays an error message indicating that the email address is already associated with an active account (MSG04). 2\. The use case continues from step 3 of the Normal Flow. **UC-7.0. E2 Invalid data or password mismatch** 1\. If required information is missing, the system displays a required-field validation message (MSG02). 2\. If the submitted data is invalid or the password confirmation does not match, the system displays a validation error message (MSG03). 3\. The use case continues from step 3 of the Normal Flow. |                   |                         |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |                         |
| Frequency of Use:  | High. Used whenever a Guest creates an account.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |                         |
| Business Rules:    | BR-04, BR-05, BR-06, BR-07, DI-01, DI-02, SEC-01.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |                         |
| Other Information: | Registration may trigger verification email based on security settings.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |                         |
| Assumptions:       | Supabase Authentication and local profile storage are available.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |                         |

####

#### **_2.2.2 Log in with account_**

| ID and Name:       | UC-08 Log in with account                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |                         |
| :----------------- | :-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :---------------------- |
| Created By:        | Phạm Minh Hải                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       | Date Created:     | 20/5/2026               |
| Primary Actor:     | Guest                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               | Secondary Actors: | Supabase Authentication |
| Description:       | As a Guest, I want to log in with my registered account credentials so that I can access the platform according to my assigned role.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |                         |
| Trigger:           | The user clicks the "Log In" or "Sign In" button.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |                         |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Guest has a registered and active account in the system. PRE-2. The Guest is not currently logged into an active session. PRE-3. Supabase Authentication is available.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |                         |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The system creates a valid authentication session or generates a secure token. POST-2. The system updates the user interface to show the authenticated state. POST-3. The user is redirected to the appropriate landing page or dashboard based on their role.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |                         |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-08.0 Log In With Account** 1\. The user opens the Login page. 2\. The system displays fields for email/username and password. 3\. The user enters credentials and submits. 4\. The system validates input format. 5\. Supabase Authentication verifies the credentials and session policy. 6\. The system reads account status and active role. 7\. The system displays MSG07 and redirects the user to the proper dashboard. 8\. The system redirects the user to the proper dashboard based on the authenticated role.                                                                       |                   |                         |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-08.1 Remember Me** 1\. At step 3 of the Normal Flow, the Guest selects Remember Me before submitting credentials. 2\. The system applies the configured persistent session policy after successful authentication. 3\. The flow continues from step 5 of the Normal Flow.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |                         |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-08.0.E1 Incorrect Credentials** 1\. At step 5, the system rejects the credentials. 2\. The system displays MSG05 and clears the password field. 3\. The use case continues from step 3 of the Normal Flow. **UC-08.0.E2 Account Temporarily Locked** 1\. At step 5 or step 6, the system detects that the failed-login threshold has been reached. 2\. The system displays MSG06. 3\. The use case ends. **UC-08.0.E3 Account Inactive, Suspended, Banned, or Deleted** 1\. At step 6, the system detects an unavailable account status. 2\. The system displays MSG11. 3\. The use case ends. |                   |                         |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |                         |
| Frequency of Use:  | Very High. Used by all active roles to access protected features.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |                         |
| Business Rules:    | BR-06, BR-07, BR-08, BR-11, BR-12                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |                         |
| Other Information: | Session timeout and failed-login limit should be configurable .                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |                         |
| Assumptions:       | The system maps authenticated identity to local account role and status correctly .                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |                         |

####

#### **_2.2.3 Log in with Google_** {#2.2.3-log-in-with-google}

| ID and Name:       | UC-09 Log in with Google                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |                         |
| :----------------- | :-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :---------------------- |
| Created By:        | Phạm Minh Hải                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 | Date Created:     | 25/5/2026               |
| Primary Actor:     | Guest                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         | Secondary Actors: | Supabase Authentication |
| Description:       | As a Guest, I want to log in using my Google account so that I can access the platform conveniently without manually entering platform credentials.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |                         |
| Trigger:           | The user clicks the "Continue with Google" or "Log in with Google" button on the authentication interface.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |                         |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The user has access to a Google account. PRE-2. OAuth communication and Supabase Authentication are available.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |                         |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The user is authenticated with a secure session token. POST-2. A matching local profile is retrieved or created. POST-3. The user is redirected to a role-based dashboard.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |                         |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-09.0 Log In With Google** 1\. The user clicks Log in with Google. 2\. The system redirects the browser to the Google OAuth endpoint. 3\. The user selects a Google account and grants required permissions. 4\. Google returns an authorization response to the system callback handler. 5\. The system relays the response to Supabase Authentication for verification. 6\. The system checks for an existing account matching the verified Google email. 7\. The system retrieves the profile, displays MSG07, and redirects the user. |                   |                         |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-09.1 First-Time Registration via Google** 1\. No local account matches the verified Google email. 2\. The system creates a local platform account using approved Google metadata. 3\. The system assigns the default role according to account rules, normally Learner. 4\. The system displays MSG07 and opens onboarding or the learner dashboard.                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |                         |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-09.0.E1 Authorization Cancelled** 1\. The user cancels the Google consent screen. 2\. The system aborts the OAuth handshake. 3\. The system returns the user to the login page without creating a session. **UC-09.0.E2 Token Verification Failure** 1\. Supabase Authentication rejects the OAuth response as invalid, expired, or corrupted. 2\. The system displays MSG03. 3\. The use case ends.                                                                                                                                     |                   |                         |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |                         |
| Frequency of Use:  | High. Expected to be a frequent login path.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |                         |
| Business Rules:    | BR-07, BR-09, BR-11, SEC-01, SEC-02                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |                         |
| Other Information: | The system must link by verified email and must not create duplicate accounts.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |                         |
| Assumptions:       | The browser supports OAuth redirects and cookies.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |                         |
