#### **_2.2.4 Forgot password_**

| ID and Name:       | UC-10 Forgot password                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |               |
| :----------------- | :--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :------------ |
| Created By:        | Phạm Minh Hải                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              | Date Created:     | 20/5/2026     |
| Primary Actor:     | Guest                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      | Secondary Actors: | Email Service |
| Description:       | As a Guest who owns a registered account, I want to reset my password when I forget it so that I can recover access to my account securely.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |               |
| Trigger:           | The user clicks the "Forgot Password" link on the login interface.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |               |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The user has a registered account associated with a valid email address. PRE-2. The system's identity and communication modules are online and functional.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |               |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The password is securely updated after a valid reset. POST-2. The reset token is invalidated after use. POST-3. The user can authenticate with the new password.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |               |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-10.0 Forgot password** 1\. The user clicks the "Forgot Password" link on the Login page. 2\. The system displays a form requesting the user's registered email address. 3\. The user enters their email address and clicks the "Send Reset Link" button. 4\. The system validates the input format, verifies the email exists in the database, and generates a secure, time-limited reset token. 5\. The system requests the Email Service to send an email containing the password reset link to the user and displays a password reset email notification (MSG09). 6\. The user clicks the reset link received in their email and is redirected to the system's "Reset Password" page. 7\. The system displays fields for entering and confirming a new password. 8\. The user enters a new password, confirms it, clicks the "Reset Password" button. 9\. The system validates the new password guidelines, updates the database, and redirects the user to the Login page with a success message. |                   |               |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-10.1 Cancel Password Reset** 1\. At step 3 or step 8 of the Normal Flow, the user clicks the "Cancel" button. 2\. The system terminates the password reset process without changing any data. 3\. The system redirects the user back to the Login page.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |               |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-10.0. E1 Email address not found** 1\. At step 4, the system detects that the entered email address is not registered. 2\. The system displays a validation error message (MSG03). 3\. The use case continues from step 3 of the Normal Flow. **UC-10.0. E2 Invalid or expired reset link** 1\. At step 6, the system detects that the token inside the reset link is invalid or has expired. 2\. The system displays a validation error message (MSG03). 3\. The use case ends without changing any data. **UC-10.0. E3 Password complexity failure** 1\. At step 9, the system detects that the passwords do not match or fail to meet the platform's complexity requirements. 2\. The system displays targeted validation error messages (MSG03). 3\. The use case continues from step 8 of the Normal Flow.                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |               |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |               |
| Frequency of Use:  | Medium. Used when users recover account access.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |               |
| Business Rules:    | BR-06, BR-07, BR-10, SEC-03, DI-01, MAI-03                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |               |
| Other Information: | This use case extends the UC-08 Log in account at the "Forgot Password" extension point on the login screen.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |               |
| Assumptions:       | The external Email Service is available and capable of delivering system emails to the user's inbox reliably.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |               |

#### **_2.2.5 Log out account_** {#2.2.5-log-out-account}

| ID and Name:       | UC-11 Log out account                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |                         |
| :----------------- | :-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :---------------------- |
| Created By:        | Phạm Minh Hải                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 | Date Created:     | 25/5/2026               |
| Primary Actor:     | Learner, Teacher, Admin                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       | Secondary Actors: | Supabase Authentication |
| Description:       | As an authenticated user, I want to log out from my current session so that I can protect my account from unauthorized access.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |                         |
| Trigger:           | The user clicks the "Log out" button.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |                         |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The user is logged into the platform with an active session.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |                         |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The active session is terminated securely. POST-2. Local authentication tokens and cookies are completely cleared from the client browser. POST-3. The user is redirected to the platform landing page.                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |                         |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-11.0 Log out account** 1\. The user clicks the "Log out" button in the navigation header or profile menu. 2\. The system triggers a sign-out request to Supabase Authentication. 3\. Supabase Authentication invalidates the current user session token. 4\. The system clears all stored auth tokens and cookies from the client side. 5\. The system redirects the user to the Homepage with a successful logout notification (MSG08). |                   |                         |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-11.1 Cancel Logout** 1\. At step 2 of the Normal Flow, the user clicks the "Cancel" button. 2\. The system closes the confirmation modal without breaking the session. 3\. The user is returned to their previous active page state.                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |                         |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-11.0 E1 Network connection failure** 1\. At step 2, the system cannot reach Supabase Authentication due to a network disruption. 2\. The system clears local client storage regardless, informs the user they have been logged out locally (MSG08), and redirects them to the Login page.                                                                                                                                                |                   |                         |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |                         |
| Frequency of Use:  | Medium. Used when users end their session.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |                         |
| Business Rules:    | BR-07, SEC-01                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |                         |
| Other Information: | Logout must invalidate the active session and clear local tokens.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |                         |
| Assumptions:       | The browser allows the platform to clear local session data.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |                         |

#### **_2.2.8 Change password_** {#2.2.8-change-password}

| ID and Name:       | UC-14 Change password                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |                         |
| :----------------- | :--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :---------------------- |
| Created By:        | Phạm Minh Hải                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              | Date Created:     | 25/5/2026               |

| Description:       | As an authenticated user, I want to change my password so that I can maintain the security of my account.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |                         |
| Trigger:           | The user selects the "Change Password" option tab from the profile setup panel.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |                         |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The user is logged in and safely inside their profile settings module (UC-12).                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |                         |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The account's secure credential metadata is updated inside Supabase Auth. POST-2. The old password is deleted and ceases to grant interface access.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |                         |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-14.0 Change Password** 1\. The user navigates and opens the "Change Password" form tab. 2\. The system exhibits inputs requiring the Current Password, New Password, and Confirm New Password. 3\. The user types matching credential information fields and clicks the "Update Password" action controller. 4\. The system validates that the target New Password field satisfies length/complexity standards and matches cleanly against the Confirm New Password field. 5\. The system relays the credentials to Supabase Authentication to verify the existing password and authorize the replacement value. 6\. Supabase Authentication processes the credential change and delivers a validation success packet back. 7\. The system empties the entry inputs, switches focus views away, and provides a password-updated notification popup.                                                                                                   |                   |                         |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-14.1 Cancel Password Change** 1\. At step 3 of the Normal Flow, the user selects the "Cancel" option button. 2\. The system resets input values inside the form modules and drops validation states. 3\. The user is redirected back to the primary account overview layout.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |                         |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-14.0. E1 Incorrect Current Password** 1\. At step 6, Supabase Authentication flags a validation rejection because the typed current password string fails matching evaluation rules. 2\. The system yields an error alert message (MSG03). 3\. The system preserves the entered new parameters and resets structural execution states to step 3\. **UC-14.0. E2 Password Fields Mismatch** 1\. At step 4, evaluation routines show mismatched string details between New Password and Confirm New Password. 2\. The system highlights mismatch alerts and halts background processing pipelines (MSG03). 3\. The workflow reverts directly to step 3\. **UC-14.0. E3 Weak Password Rejection** 1\. At step 4, checks identify that the selected password string fails basic security strength requirements. 2\. The system provides password complexity rules and requirements underneath the input box (MSG03). 3\. The workflow returns to step 3\. |                   |                         |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |                         |
| Frequency of Use:  | Low to Medium. Used for routine security updates or credential risk.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |                         |
| Business Rules:    | BR-06, BR-07, BR-14, SEC-03, DI-01                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |                         |
| Other Information: | Password policy should be configurable and enforced before update.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |                         |
| Assumptions:       | The external authentication system is fully operational and capable of updating security parameters in real time.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |                         |

#### **_2.2.9 Switch account role_** {#2.2.9-switch-account-role}

| ID and Name:       | UC-15 Switch account role                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |            |
| :----------------- | :------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | :---------------- | :--------- |
| Created By:        | Phạm Minh Hải                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     | Date Created:     | 03/06/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Learner, Teacher                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | Secondary Actors: | None       |
| Description:       | As a Learner or Teacher, I want to switch my active role between Learner and Teacher so that I can use learning features or teaching features within the same account without creating another account.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |            |
| Trigger:           | The Learner or Teacher clicks the “Switch Role” option.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |            |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The user is authenticated. PRE-2. The account is active and allowed to switch role. PRE-3. The current account is not an Admin-only account for this action.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |            |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The active role is updated. POST-2. Permissions and navigation are refreshed. POST-3. The user is redirected to the corresponding dashboard. POST-4. Existing learning, teaching, payment, and reporting data are preserved.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |            |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-15.0 Switch Account Role** 1\. The user opens the profile or dashboard menu. 2\. The system displays the current active role. 3\. The user clicks Switch Role. 4\. The system displays available target role options. 5\. The user selects Learner or Teacher. 6\. The system asks for confirmation. 7\. The user confirms. 8\. The system validates the authentication session and account status. 9\. The system updates the active role. 10\. The system refreshes permission scope and navigation. 11\. The system displays a success message and redirects to the corresponding dashboard.                                                                                                                                              |                   |            |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-15.1 Switch Learner to Teacher** 1\. The current active role is Learner. 2\. The user selects Teacher. 3\. The system updates active role to Teacher and opens the Teacher Dashboard. **UC-15.2 Switch Teacher to Learner** 1\. The current active role is Teacher. 2\. The user selects Learner. 3\. The system updates active role to Learner and opens the Learner Dashboard. **UC-15.3 Cancel Role Switch** 1\. The user cancels the confirmation. 2\. The system keeps the current role unchanged. 3\. The user remains on the previous page.                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |            |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-15.0.E1 User Not Authenticated** 1\. The system detects no valid session or an expired session. 2\. The system displays MSG50 and redirects to Login. **UC-15.0.E2 Account Not Allowed** 1\. The system detects the account is locked, suspended, banned, deleted, or inactive. 2\. The system displays MSG11. 3\. The use case ends. **UC-15.0.E3 Target Role Same as Current Role** 1\. The system detects that the selected target role is already active. 2\. The system displays an informational notification. 3\. The role remains unchanged. **UC-15.0.E4 Role Switch Failed** 1\. The system cannot update the active role due to database or network error. 2\. The system displays MSG13. 3\. The current role remains unchanged. |                   |            |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |            |
| Frequency of Use:  | Medium. Used when users move between learning and teaching workflows.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |            |
| Business Rules:    | BR-07, BR-11, BR-12, BR-13, SEC-02, DI-04                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |            |
| Other Information: | Admin access must not be granted through role switching.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |            |
| Assumptions:       | Active role is stored separately from account identity and historical data.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |            |

### **2.3 Class management** {#2.3-class-management}

#### **_2.3.1 View joined classes_** {#2.3.1-view-joined-classes}

| ID and Name:       | UC-17 View joined classes                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Vũ Đình Thái                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             | Date Created:     | 24/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Learner                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | Secondary Actors: |           |
| Description:       | As a Learner, I want to view my joined classes so that I can access assigned study sets, available exams, class information, and teacher activities.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The Learner clicks the “My Classes” or “Joined Classes” menu from the learner dashboard.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Learner has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The Learner account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The Class Management module is available.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The system displays the list of classes joined by the Learner. POST-2. The Learner can select a class to view its details, assigned study sets, or available exams. POST-3. No class membership data is changed by this use case.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-17.0 View Joined Classes** 1\. The Learner opens the “My Classes” page. 2\. The system retrieves all classes where the Learner is an approved member. 3\. The system displays the joined class list with basic information such as class name, teacher name, subject, class code, number of members, and class status. 4\. The Learner reviews the joined class list. 5\. The Learner selects a class from the list. 6\. The system displays the selected class detail page.        |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-17.1 Search or Filter Joined Classes** 1\. The Learner enters a keyword or selects a filter such as subject, teacher, or class status. 2\. The system applies the search or filter criteria. 3\. The system displays matching joined classes. **UC-17.2 Empty Joined Class List** 1\. The system finds that the Learner has not joined any class. 2\. The system displays an empty state message. 3\. The system may suggest joining a class using a class code or invitation link. |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-17.0. E1 Data Retrieval Error** 1\. The system cannot retrieve class data due to a system or network error. 2\. The system displays an error message (MSG13). 3\. The use case ends.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | High. Learners frequently access their joined classes to study assigned materials and participate in exams.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |           |
| Business Rules     | BR-01, BR-07, BR-09, BR-13, BR-14                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |           |
| Other Information: | The joined class list should support pagination or sorting if the Learner belongs to many classes.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The system correctly stores class membership status and only displays classes where the Learner has been approved or successfully added.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |           |

#### **_2.3.2 Join class_** {#2.3.2-join-class}

| ID and Name:       | UC-18 Join class                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Vũ Đình Thái                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       | Date Created:     | 24/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Learner                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            | Secondary Actors: |           |
| Description:       | As a Learner, I want to join a class using a class code or invitation link so that I can access learning materials, study sets, and exams assigned by the Teacher.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The Learner enters a class code, opens an invitation link, or clicks the “Join Class” button.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Learner has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The Learner account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The class code or invitation link exists in the system. PRE-4. The target class is active and allows learners to join.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. A class join request is created, or the Learner is added to the class according to the class joining rule. POST-2. The Learner can view the join request status if approval is required. POST-3. If auto-approval is enabled, the class appears in the Learner’s joined class list.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | UC-18.0 Join Class 1\. The Learner opens the “Join Class” page. 2\. The system displays the class code input field. 3\. The Learner enters a class code. 4\. The system validates the class code. 5\. The system checks whether the class is active and available for joining. 6\. The system checks whether the Learner is already a member of the class or already has a pending join request. 7\. The system creates a join request for the class. 8\. The system displays a join request success message (MSG19). 9\. The Learner views the request status.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-18.1 Auto-Approved Class Join** 1\. At step 8 of the Normal Flow, the system detects that the class allows automatic joining. 2\. The system adds the Learner directly to the class member list. 3\. The system displays a join request success message (MSG19). 4\. The class appears in the Learner’s joined class list **UC-18.2 Join by Invitation Link** 1\. The Learner opens a valid class invitation link. 2\. The system validates the invitation link and target class. 3\. The system checks whether the Learner is already a member of the class or already has a pending join request. 4\. The system creates a join request or directly adds the Learner according to the class joining rule. 5\. The system displays a join request success message (MSG19). 6\. The Learner views the request status or the joined class detail page.**UC-18.3 Cancel Join Class** 1\. Before submitting the class code, the Learner clicks “Cancel”. 2\. The system cancels the operation. 3\. The system redirects the Learner back to the class list page. |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-18.0. E1 Class Not Found** 1\. The system cannot find a class matching the submitted code or invitation link. 2\. The system displays a validation error message (MSG03). 3\. The use case ends. **UC-18.0. E2 Class Is Closed or Inactive** 1\. The system detects that the class is closed, archived, or no longer accepting new members. 2\. The system displays a permission error message (MSG11). 3\. The use case ends. **UC-18.0. E3 Already Joined or Already Requested** 1\. The system detects that the Learner is already a class member or already has a pending request. 2\. The system displays an already-member notification (MSG20). 3\. The use case ends.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | High. Learners use this feature whenever they need to join a new class created by a Teacher.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Business Rules     | BR-01, BR-07, BR-09, BR-12, BR-13, BR-14, BR-35                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |           |
| Other Information: | The system may notify the Teacher when a new join request is submitted.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | Each class has a unique class code or invitation token generated by the system.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |           |
