#### **_2.3.4 Create class_** {#2.3.4-create-class}

| ID and Name:       | UC-29 Create class                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Vũ Đình Thái                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              | Date Created:     | 24/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Teacher                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   | Secondary Actors: |           |
| Description:       | As a Teacher, I want to create a new online class so that Learners can join and receive assigned study sets, practice tasks, and exam sessions.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The Teacher clicks the “Create Class” button from the Class Management page.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Teacher has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The Teacher account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The Teacher has permission to create classes. PRE-4. The Class Management module is available.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. A new class is created and saved in the system. POST-2. The new class is linked to the Teacher as its owner or manager. POST-3. The system generates a unique class code or invitation link for the class. POST-4. The Teacher can manage learners, assign study sets, and configure exam sessions for the class.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-29.0 Create Class** 1\. The Teacher goes to the Class Management page. 2\. The Teacher clicks the “Create Class” button. 3\. The system displays the Create Class form. 4\. The Teacher enters class information such as class name, subject, description, semester, grade level, and joining rule. 5\. The Teacher submits the form. 6\. The system validates the required class information. 7\. The system generates a unique class code or invitation link. 8\. The system saves the new class to the system. 9\. The system displays a class creation success message (MSG21). 10\. The system redirects the Teacher to the new class detail page.                                                                                                                                              |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-29.1 Create Class with Minimal Information** 1\. At step 4 of the Normal Flow, the Teacher enters only required information. 2\. The system validates that all required information is provided. 3\. The system saves the class with optional fields left empty or set to default values. 4\. The flow continues from step 7 of the Normal Flow and displays a class creation success message (MSG21). **UC-29.2 Cancel Create Class** 1\. Before submitting the form, the Teacher clicks “Cancel”. 2\. The system discards all entered data. 3\. The system redirects the Teacher back to the class list page.                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-29.0. E1 Missing Required Information** 1\. The system detects that required fields are missing. 2\. The system displays a required-field validation message (MSG02). 3\. The Teacher corrects the information or cancels the action. **UC-29.0. E2 Invalid Input** 1\. The system detects invalid input such as unsupported characters or text exceeding the allowed length. 2\. The system displays a validation error message (MSG03). 3\. The Teacher corrects the input or cancels the action. **UC-29.0. E3 Duplicate Class Name** 1\. The system detects that the Teacher already has a class with the same name, if duplicate checking is enabled. 2\. The system displays a validation error message (MSG03). 3\. The Teacher changes the class name or confirms according to system rules. |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | High. Teachers create classes when setting up new learning groups, courses, or exam groups.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| Business Rules     | BR-01, BR-07, BR-09, BR-11, BR-12, BR-14, BR-15                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |           |
| Other Information: | A newly created class may have no learners, study sets, or exams until the Teacher configures them.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The Teacher understands the class information and joining rule before creating the class.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |           |

#### **_2.3.6 Approve class join request_** {#2.3.6-approve-class-join-request}

| ID and Name:       | UC-31 Approve class join request                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |               |
| :----------------- | :-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :------------ |
| Created By:        | Vũ Đình Thái                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | Date Created:     | 24/5/2026     |
| Primary Actor:     | Teacher                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     | Secondary Actors: | Email Service |
| Description:       | As a Teacher, I want to approve Learners’ class join requests so that only accepted Learners can access class learning activities.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |               |
| Trigger:           | The Teacher opens the pending join requests list and clicks “Approve” for a specific request.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |               |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Teacher has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The Teacher account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The selected class exists in the system. PRE-4. The Teacher owns or has permission to manage the selected class. PRE-5. The join request exists and is currently pending.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |               |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The selected join request is approved. POST-2. The Learner is added to the class member list. POST-3. The Learner can access class materials, assigned study sets, and available exams according to class rules. POST-4. The system may notify the Learner about the approval result.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |               |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-31.0 Approve Class Join Request** 1\. The Teacher goes to a class detail page. 2\. The Teacher opens the “Join Requests” section. 3\. The system displays pending join requests. 4\. The Teacher selects a pending request and clicks “Approve”. 5\. The system validates that the request is still pending. 6\. The system updates the request status to “Approved”. 7\. The system adds the Learner to the class member list. 8\. The system displays a class join approval success message (MSG22). 9\. The system may send a notification or email to the Learner. |                   |               |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-31.1 Reject Join Request** 1\. At step 8 of the Normal Flow, the Teacher clicks “Reject” instead of “Approve”. 2\. The system updates the request status to “Rejected”. 3\. The system does not add the Learner to the class. 4\. The system displays a success message. 5\. The system may notify the Learner of the rejection.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |               |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-31.0. E1 Join Request Not Found** 1\. The system cannot find the selected join request. 2\. The system displays a validation error message (MSG03). 3\. The use case ends. **UC-31.0. E2 Request Already Processed** 1\. The system detects that the request has already been approved, rejected, or cancelled. 2\. The system displays the current request status. 3\. The use case ends. **UC-31.0. E3 Approval Failed** 1\. The system fails to approve the request due to a system or network error. 2\. The system displays a system unavailable message (MSG41). |                   |               |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |               |
| Frequency of Use:  | Medium to High. Teachers use this feature whenever Learners request to join classes requiring approval.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |               |
| Business Rules     | BR-01, BR-07, BR-09, BR-11, BR-13, BR-14, BR-15, BR-35                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |               |
| Other Information: | The system should prevent duplicate class membership when approving a join request.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |               |
| Assumptions:       | The Teacher can identify whether the requesting Learner should be allowed to join the class.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |               |

#### **_2.3.7 Remove learner from class_** {#2.3.7-remove-learner-from-class}

| ID and Name:       | UC-32 Remove learner from class                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Vũ Đình Thái                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      | Date Created:     | 24/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Teacher                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           | Secondary Actors: |           |
| Description:       | As a Teacher, I want to remove a Learner from a class so that I can manage class membership accurately.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The Teacher clicks the “Remove” button for a Learner in the class member list.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Teacher has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The Teacher account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The selected class exists in the system. PRE-4. The Teacher owns or has permission to manage the selected class. PRE-5. The selected Learner is currently a member of the class.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The selected Learner is removed from the class member list. POST-2. The removed Learner can no longer access class-only study sets, exams, and class activities unless re-added. POST-3. Historical learning records, exam attempts, and reports remain preserved if required by system rules.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-32.0 Remove learner from Class** 1\. The Teacher goes to a class detail page. 2\. The Teacher opens the “Members” tab. 3\. The system displays the class member list. 4\. The Teacher selects a Learner and clicks “Remove”. 5\. The system displays a removal confirmation message. 6\. The Teacher confirms the removal. 7\. The system removes the Learner from the class but preserves historical records for reports and audit purposes. 8\. The system displays a learner removal success message (MSG23), and displays the updated class member list. |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-32.1 Cancel Removal** 1\. At step 9 of the Normal Flow, the Teacher clicks “Cancel”. 2\. The system cancels the removal action. 3\. The system returns the Teacher to the member list.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-32.0. E4 Learner Not Found in Class** 1\. The system detects that the selected Learner is not currently a member of the class. 2\. The system displays a validation error message (MSG03). 3\. The use case ends. **UC-32.0. E6 Remove Failed** 1\. The system fails to remove the Learner due to a system or network error. 2\. The system displays a system unavailable message (MSG41). 3\. The class membership remains unchanged.                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Priority:          | Medium                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | Medium. Teachers use this feature occasionally to manage incorrect, inactive, or unauthorized class members.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |
| Business Rules     | BR-01, BR-07, BR-09, BR-11, BR-15, BR-22, BR-27, BR-34                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| Other Information: | The system should prefer removing the Learner from active membership while preserving historical learning and exam records for reporting consistency.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The Teacher understands that removing a Learner may affect the Learner’s future access to class-only resources and exam sessions.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |           |

### **2.4 Question Management & Question Bank Repository** {#2.4-question-management-&-question-bank-repository}

#### **_2.4.1 View question banks_** {#2.4.1-view-question-banks}

| ID and Name:       | UC-33 View question banks                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Nguyễn Khắc Thành Sơn                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   | Date Created:     | 20/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Teacher                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 | Secondary Actors: |           |
| Description:       | As a Teacher, I want to view the Question Banks that I own or am authorized to access so that I can reuse stored questions for Study Set or Exam creation.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The Teacher clicks the Question Banks menu or opens the Question Bank Repository page.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Teacher has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The Teacher account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The active role is Teacher.PRE-4. The Question Bank Repository module is available.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The system displays the Question Banks owned by or authorized for the Teacher. POST-2. The Teacher can select a Question Bank to manage metadata, author questions, or reuse questions for Study Set or Exam creation.POST-3. Learners and Guests do not gain direct access to any Question Bank.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-33.0 View Question Banks** 1\. The Teacher opens the Question Banks page. 2\. The system validates that the current user is authenticated, active, and using the Teacher role. 3\. The system retrieves Question Banks owned by or authorized for the Teacher. 4\. The system displays repository information such as title, description, subject, visibility, owner, question count, and last updated time. 5\. The Teacher searches, filters, or sorts the Question Bank list if needed. 6\. The Teacher selects a Question Bank to view its detail page. |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-33.1 No Question Banks Available**1\. At step 3 of the Normal Flow, the system finds no available Question Bank. 2\. The system displays a no matching data message (MSG45). 3\. The system provides the Create Question Bank action. 4\. The Teacher may proceed to UC-34 Create question bank.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-33.0.E1 Unauthorized Access** 1\. At step 2 of the Normal Flow, the system detects that the user does not have permission to access Teacher Question Bank functions. 2\. The system displays a permission error message (MSG11). 3\. The use case ends. **UC-33.0.E2 Load Failure** 1\. At step 3 of the Normal Flow, the system cannot load Question Bank data due to a network or system error. 2\. The system displays a data loading failure message (MSG13). 3\. The use case ends.                                                                           |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | Medium. Teachers use this feature when maintaining reusable question repositories or preparing Study Sets and Exam Sessions.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| Business Rules     | BR-07, BR-11, BR-12, BR-28                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |           |
| Other Information: | Question Banks are internal Teacher repositories and are not searchable through public discovery.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The system can determine Question Bank ownership and authorization scope for each Teacher.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |           |

#### **_2.4.2 Create question bank_** {#2.4.2-create-question-bank}

| ID and Name:       | UC-34 Create question bank                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Nguyễn Khắc Thành Sơn                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               | Date Created:     | 20/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Teacher                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             | Secondary Actors: |           |
| Description:       | As a Teacher, I want to create a Question Bank as a reusable repository so that I can store questions for repeated Study Set or Exam creation.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The Teacher clicks the Create Question Bank button.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Teacher has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The Teacher account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The active role is Teacher. PRE-4. The Teacher has permission to create a Question Bank.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. A new Question Bank is created and saved in the system. POST-2. The new Question Bank is linked to the Teacher as its owner. POST-3. The new Question Bank is displayed in the Teacher’s Question Bank list. POST-4. If the creation fails or is cancelled, no new Question Bank is saved.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-34.0 Create Question Bank** 1\. The Teacher opens the Question Banks page. 2\. The Teacher clicks Create Question Bank. 3\. The system displays the Create Question Bank form. 4\. The Teacher enters required repository information such as title, description, subject, visibility, and repository configuration. 5\. The Teacher submits the form. 6\. The system validates the required repository information and Teacher authorization. 7\. The system creates the Question Bank. 8\. The system displays a question bank saved success message (MSG25). 9\. The system opens the new Question Bank detail page. |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-34.1 Cancel Creation** 1\. At step 4 of the Normal Flow, the Teacher clicks Cancel. 2\. The system discards unsaved data. 3\. The system returns the Teacher to the Question Banks page. 4\. No new Question Bank is saved.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-34.0.E1 Missing Required Information** 1\. At step 6 of the Normal Flow, the system detects that required Question Bank information is missing. 2\. The system displays a required information message (MSG02). 3\. The Teacher corrects the information. 4\. The flow continues from step 4 of the Normal Flow. **UC-34.0.E2 Invalid Repository Data** 1\. At step 6 of the Normal Flow, the system detects invalid repository information. 2\. The system displays an invalid information message (MSG03). 3\. The Teacher corrects the information. 4\. The flow continues from step 4 of the Normal Flow.                  |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | Medium. Teachers create repositories when preparing repeated learning or exam materials.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-07, BR-11, BR-12, BR-28, BR-29                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |
| Other Information: | Creating a Question Bank creates repository metadata only. Question content is added through shared Question Management.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The system supports empty Question Banks and allows questions to be added later.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |           |

#### **_2.4.3 Update question bank information_** {#2.4.3-update-question-bank-information}

| ID and Name:       | UC-35 Update question bank information                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Vũ Đình Thái                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        | Date Created:     | 20/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Teacher                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             | Secondary Actors: |           |
| Description:       | As a Teacher, I want to update Question Bank information so that repository metadata remains accurate and useful for future reuse.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The Teacher clicks the “Edit” or “Update Question Bank” button on a question bank detail page.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Teacher has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The Teacher account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The active role is Teacher. PRE-4. The selected Question Bank exists. PRE-5. The Teacher owns or is authorized to update the selected Question Bank.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The selected Question Bank metadata is updated successfully. POST-2. Existing questions inside the Question Bank remain unchanged unless the Teacher uses Question Management use cases. POST-3. Learners and Guests do not gain direct access to the Question Bank. POST-4. If the update fails or is cancelled, the original Question Bank information remains unchanged.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-35.0 Update Question Bank Information** 1\. The Teacher opens an authorized Question Bank detail page. 2\. The Teacher clicks Edit or Update Question Bank. 3\. The system displays existing repository metadata. 4\. The Teacher updates title, description, subject, visibility, or repository configuration. 5\. The Teacher submits the updated metadata. 6\. The system validates the updated data and Teacher authorization. 7\. The system saves the changes. 8\. The system displays a question bank saved success message (MSG25). 9\. The system displays the updated Question Bank detail page.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-35.1 Cancel Update** 1\. At step 4 of the Normal Flow, the Teacher clicks Cancel. 2\. The system discards unsaved changes. 3\. The system returns the Teacher to the Question Bank detail page. 4\. The original Question Bank information remains unchanged.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-35.0.E1 Missing Required Information** 1\. At step 6 of the Normal Flow, the system detects missing required Question Bank information. 2\. The system displays a required information message (MSG02). 3\. The Teacher corrects the information. 4\. The flow continues from step 4 of the Normal Flow. **UC-35.0.E2 Invalid Metadata** 1\. At step 6 of the Normal Flow, the system detects invalid metadata. 2\. The system displays an invalid information message (MSG03). 3\. The Teacher corrects the information. 4\. The flow continues from step 4 of the Normal Flow. **UC-35.0.E3 Unauthorized Repository** 1\. At step 6 of the Normal Flow, the system detects that the Teacher is not authorized to update the selected Question Bank. 2\. The system blocks the update and displays a permission error message (MSG11). 3\. The use case ends. |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | Medium. Teachers use this feature when maintaining reusable repository information.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-07, BR-11, BR-12, BR-28, BR-29                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |
| Other Information: | This use case updates repository metadata only.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The system can separate repository metadata changes from question content changes.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |

#### **_2.4.4 Delete question bank_** {#2.4.4-delete-question-bank}

| ID and Name:       | UC-36 Delete question bank                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Vũ Đình Thái                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 | Date Created:     | 20/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Teacher                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      | Secondary Actors: |           |
| Description:       | As a Teacher, I want to delete, archive, or hide a Question Bank that is no longer needed while preserving historical learning, exam, and reporting integrity.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The Teacher clicks Delete, Archive, or Hide on a Question Bank detail page.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Teacher has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The Teacher account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The active role is Teacher. PRE-4. The selected Question Bank exists. PRE-5. The Teacher owns or is authorized to delete, archive, or hide the selected Question Bank.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The Question Bank is deleted, archived, hidden, or deactivated according to integrity rules. POST-2. Historical exam, learning, and report records remain valid. POST-3. Study Sets created from copied Question Bank questions are not deleted automatically. POST-4. If the action fails or is cancelled, the Question Bank remains unchanged.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-36.0 Delete Question Bank** 1\. The Teacher opens an authorized Question Bank detail page. 2\. The Teacher clicks Delete, Archive, or Hide. 3\. The system displays a confirmation message. 4\. The Teacher confirms the action. 5\. The system checks ownership, authorization, and references from Study Sets, Exam Sessions, reports, or historical records. 6\. The system determines the allowed action according to integrity rules. 7\. If hard deletion is allowed, the system deletes the Question Bank. 8\. If hard deletion is not allowed but archive or hide is allowed, the system archives or hides the Question Bank instead. 9\. The system displays the updated Question Bank status. 10\. The system returns the Teacher to the Question Banks page. |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-36.1 Cancel Deletion** 1\. At step 3 of the Normal Flow, the Teacher cancels the confirmation. 2\. The system closes the confirmation message. 3\. The Question Bank remains unchanged.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-36.0.E1 Unauthorized Action** 1\. At step 5 of the Normal Flow, the system detects that the Teacher is not authorized to delete, archive, or hide the Question Bank. 2\. The system blocks the action and displays a permission error message (MSG11). 3\. The Question Bank remains unchanged. **UC-36.0.E2 System Failure** 1\. At step 7 or step 8 of the Normal Flow, the system fails to update the Question Bank status. 2\. The system displays a data loading or system error message (MSG13). 3\. The Question Bank remains unchanged.                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |           |
| Priority:          | Medium                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | Medium. Teachers use this feature when cleaning up unused repositories                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-07, BR-11, BR-12, BR-28, BR-30                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
