| Other Information: | Deleting a Question Bank must not remove copied question content already stored in Study Sets or historical Exam Sessions.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The system supports archive or hide behavior when hard deletion is unsafe                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |           |

####

#### **_2.4.5 Add question manually_** {#2.4.5-add-question-manually}

| ID and Name:       | UC-37 Add question manually                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Lê Hải Đăng                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     | Date Created:     | 20/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Teacher                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         | Secondary Actors: |           |
| Description:       | As a Teacher, I want to manually add questions to owned or authorized Study Sets and Question Banks so that I can build learning or assessment content.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The Teacher clicks the Add Question action from an owned or authorized Study Set or Question Bank.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Teacher has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The Teacher account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The active role is Teacher. PRE-4. The selected Study Set or Question Bank exists. PRE-5. The Teacher owns or is authorized to manage the selected question container.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. A new question is saved into the selected authorized Study Set or Question Bank. POST-2. The question becomes available for later preview, study set learning, or exam creation according to its container. POST-3. If the action fails or is cancelled, no question is saved.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-37.0 Add Question Manually** 1\. The Teacher opens an owned or authorized Study Set or Question Bank. 2\. The Teacher clicks Add Question. 3\. The system displays the manual question form. 4\. The Teacher enters question content, answer options if required, correct answer, score, explanation, tags, and chapter where applicable. 5\. The Teacher submits the question form. 6\. The system validates Teacher authorization and required question data. 7\. The system displays the question preview before saving. 8\. The Teacher reviews the preview and confirms saving. 9\. The system saves the question into the selected authorized container. 10\. The system displays MSG29.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-37.1 Save And Add Another Question** 1\. At step 8, the Teacher selects Save and Add Another. 2\. The system saves the current question. 3\. The system displays MSG29. 4\. The system opens a new empty manual question form. 5\. The flow continues from step 4\. **UC-37.2 Cancel Manual Question Creation** 1\. At step 5 or step 8, the Teacher cancels the action. 2\. The system discards unsaved question data after confirmation. 3\. No question is saved.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-37.0.E1 Unauthorized Question Container** 1\. At step 6, the system detects that the Teacher is not authorized to add questions to the selected container. 2\. The system blocks the action and displays MSG11. **UC-37.0.E2 Missing Required Question Data** 1\. At step 6, the system detects that required question information is missing. 2\. The system highlights the missing fields and displays MSG02. 3\. The Teacher corrects the data. 4\. The flow continues from step 4\. **UC-37.0.E3 Invalid Question Data** 1\. At step 6, the system detects invalid question content, answer data, score, or classification information. 2\. The system highlights invalid fields and displays MSG03. 3\. The Teacher corrects the data. 4\. The flow continues from step 4\. **UC-37.0.E4 Preview Required** 1\. At step 8, the Teacher attempts to save without previewing the question. 2\. The system blocks saving and displays MSG31. 3\. The Teacher previews the question. 4\. The flow continues from step 8\. |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | High. Teachers use this feature frequently when creating learning and assessment content.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-11, BR-12, BR-31, BR-32, BR-34                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| Other Information: | Only Teachers can manually add questions to Question Banks. Questions may also be added to Study Sets if the Teacher owns the Study Set.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The system supports multiple question types and validates each question according to its required data structure.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |

#### **_2.4.6 Import questions from Excel_** {#2.4.6-import-questions-from-excel}

| ID and Name:       | UC-38 Import questions from Excel                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Nguyễn Khắc Thành Sơn                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           | Date Created:     | 25/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Teacher                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         | Secondary Actors: |           |
| Description:       | As a Teacher, I want to import questions from an Excel template into an owned or authorized Study Set or Question Bank so that I can create many questions efficiently.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The Teacher clicks Import Questions from an owned or authorized Study Set or Question Bank.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Teacher has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The Teacher account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The target question container exists. PRE-4. The Teacher has authoring permission for the target container. PRE-5. The Excel file follows the platform question import template.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. Valid imported questions are saved into the selected Study Set or Question Bank after Teacher approval. POST-2. Invalid rows are not saved. POST-3. Row-level errors are available for review when import validation fails. POST-4. If the import is cancelled, no imported question is saved.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-38.0 Import Questions From Excel** 1\. The Teacher opens an owned or authorized Study Set or Question Bank. 2\. The Teacher clicks Import Questions. 3\. The system displays the import form and template requirements. 4\. The Teacher selects or uploads an Excel file. 5\. The Teacher confirms the target container. 6\. The system validates file format, required columns, question content, answer options, correct answers, score, and metadata. 7\. The system separates valid rows and invalid rows. 8\. The system displays an import preview and row-level errors if any. 9\. The Teacher reviews the import result. 10\. The Teacher confirms saving valid questions. 11\. The system saves approved valid questions into the selected container. 12\. The system displays an import success message (MSG28). |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-38.1 Import Valid Rows Only** 1\. At step 8 of the Normal Flow, the system finds both valid and invalid rows. 2\. The system displays a row-level validation error message (MSG27). 3\. The Teacher chooses to save only valid rows. 4\. The system saves valid rows and keeps invalid rows unsaved. 5\. The system displays MSG28. **UC-38.2 Re-upload Corrected File** 1\. At step 8 of the Normal Flow, the Teacher reviews row-level errors. 2\. The Teacher corrects the Excel file. 3\. The Teacher uploads the corrected file. 4\. The flow continues from step 6 of the Normal Flow. **UC-38.3 Cancel Import** 1\. At step 9 of the Normal Flow, the Teacher cancels the import. 2\. The system discards the import session. 3\. No imported question is saved.                                                    |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-38.0.E1 Missing Excel File** 1\. At step 6 of the Normal Flow, the system detects that no Excel file has been uploaded. 2\. The system displays a required information message (MSG02). 3\. The Teacher uploads a file. 4\. The flow continues from step 4 of the Normal Flow. **UC-38.0.E2 Invalid Excel Template** 1\. At step 6 of the Normal Flow, the system detects that the file does not follow the required template or has an invalid format. 2\. The system displays an invalid information message (MSG03). 3\. No question is saved.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | High. Teachers import questions when preparing large Study Sets or reusable Question Banks.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-07, BR-11, BR-12, BR-31, BR-32, BR-33, BR-34                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |           |
| Other Information: | The same Excel template is used for Study Sets and Question Banks. Authorization is based on the selected target container.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The system can validate Excel files before saving any question records.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |           |

####

#### **_2.4.7 View question import errors_** {#2.4.7-view-question-import-errors}

| ID and Name:       | UC-39 View question import errors                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Nguyễn Khắc Thành Sơn                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    | Date Created:     | 25/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Teacher                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | Secondary Actors: |           |
| Description:       | As a Teacher, I want to view row-level import errors so that I can correct invalid question data before saving it into a Study Set or Question Bank.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The system detects invalid rows during Excel import and the Teacher opens the import error result.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The user has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The user has started UC-38 Import questions from Excel. PRE-3. The system has completed validation and found invalid rows. PRE-4. The user still has permission for the selected target container.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. Import errors are displayed to the user. POST-2. Invalid rows remain unsaved. POST-3. The user can correct the Excel file, re-upload it, or continue with valid rows when allowed.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | UC-39.0 View Question Import Errors 1\. The system detects invalid rows during Excel import. 2\. The system displays a row-level validation error message (MSG27). 3\. The Teacher clicks View Errors or opens the import error panel. 4\. The system displays row number, field name, invalid value, and validation reason. 5\. The Teacher reviews the error details. 6\. The Teacher decides whether to correct the file, re-upload, cancel import, or save valid rows only if allowed.                                                               |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-39.1 Filter Error List** 1\. At step 4 of the Normal Flow, the Teacher filters errors by row number, field name, or error type. 2\. The system applies the filter. 3\. If matching errors exist, the system displays the matching error list. 4\. If no matching errors exist, the system shows no matching data (MSG45). **UC-39.2 Export Error List** 1\. At step 5 of the Normal Flow, the Teacher exports or copies error details if the screen supports it. 2\. The system provides the error information for correction outside the platform. |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-39.0.E1 Import Session Expired** 1\. At step 3 of the Normal Flow, the system detects that the import session no longer exists. 2\. The system asks the Teacher to upload the Excel file again. 3\. The use case ends. **UC-39.0.E2 Unauthorized Import Result** 1\. At step 4 of the Normal Flow, the system detects that the Teacher no longer has permission for the target container. 2\. The system blocks access and displays a permission error message (MSG11). 3\. The use case ends.                                                      |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | Medium. Users view errors when imported files contain invalid rows.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-07, BR-11, BR-12, BR-31, BR-33                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |           |
| Other Information: | This use case is always connected to question import from Excel and does not save questions by itself.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The system stores temporary import validation results long enough for the Teacher to review them.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |           |

####

#### **_2.4.8 Preview questions before saving_** {#2.4.8-preview-questions-before-saving}

| ID and Name:       | UC-40 Preview questions before saving                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Nguyễn Khắc Thành Sơn                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 | Date Created:     | 25/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Teacher                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               | Secondary Actors: |           |
| Description:       | As a Teacher, I want to preview manually entered, imported, copied, or AI-generated questions before saving them so that I can confirm quality and correctness.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The system has question drafts from manual input, Excel import, Question Bank copy flow, or AI generation and the Teacher opens the preview step.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Teacher has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The Teacher account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The question draft exists. PRE-4. The target Study Set or Question Bank exists. PRE-5. The Teacher has permission to save questions into the target container.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. Approved valid questions are saved into the selected Study Set or Question Bank. POST-2. Unapproved or invalid drafts are not saved. POST-3. If the target is a Study Set, saved questions are available for learning according to access rules. POST-4. If the target is a Question Bank, saved questions become reusable repository content.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-40.0 Preview Questions Before Saving** 1\. The Teacher reaches the preview step after manual entry, Excel import, Question Bank copy selection, or AI generation. 2\. The system displays each question draft with question content, options, correct answer, explanation, score, tags, and chapter. 3\. The Teacher reviews the draft questions. 4\. The Teacher edits, removes, or confirms each draft as needed. 5\. The Teacher clicks Save Approved Questions. 6\. The system validates approved drafts and target container authorization. 7\. The system saves approved valid questions into the selected container. 8\. If the drafts are imported from Excel, the system displays an import success message (MSG28). 9\. If the drafts are manually entered, copied, or AI-generated, the system displays a question saved success message (MSG29). |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-40.1 Edit Draft In Preview** 1\. At step 4 of the Normal Flow, the Teacher edits a draft question. 2\. The system validates the edited draft. 3\. The flow continues from step 3 of the Normal Flow. **UC-40.2 Remove Draft From Preview** 1\. At step 4 of the Normal Flow, the Teacher removes a draft question. 2\. The system excludes the draft from saving. 3\. The flow continues from step 3 of the Normal Flow. **UC-40.3 Save Subset Of Drafts** 1\. At step 5 of the Normal Flow, the Teacher approves only selected drafts. 2\. The system saves only approved valid drafts. 3\. The system displays MSG28 or MSG29 depending on the source of the saved drafts.                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-40.0.E1 Preview Required** 1\. The Teacher attempts to save questions without previewing them. 2\. The system blocks saving and displays a preview required message (MSG31). 3\. The use case continues from step 1 of the Normal Flow. **UC-40.0.E2 Invalid Draft Data** 1\. At step 6 of the Normal Flow, the system detects that an approved draft is invalid. 2\. The system displays an invalid information message (MSG03). 3\. The system highlights the invalid draft and prevents it from being saved until corrected. **UC-40.0.E3 Unauthorized Target Container** 1\. At step 6 of the Normal Flow, the system detects that the Teacher cannot save questions into the target container. 2\. The system blocks saving and displays a permission error message (MSG11). 3\. No draft is saved.                                                                                         |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | High. Preview is used whenever questions are manually created, imported, copied, or generated by AI.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-07, BR-11, BR-12, BR-31, BR-32, BR-34                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |           |
| Other Information: | Preview is a shared quality gate before saving questions to either Study Sets or Question Banks.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The system can keep temporary question drafts before final save                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |

####

#### **_2.4.9 Update question_** {#2.4.9-update-question}

| ID and Name:       | UC-41 Update question                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Nguyễn Khắc Thành Sơn                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            | Date Created:     | 25/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Teacher                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          | Secondary Actors: |           |
| Description:       | As a Teacher, I want to update question content, answer options, correct answer, score, explanation, tags, or chapter inside an authorized question container so that I can correct or improve question quality.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The Teacher clicks Edit or Update Question from a Study Set question list, Study Set question detail, or Question Bank question list.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Teacher has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The Teacher account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The selected question container exists. PRE-4. The selected question exists in the container. PRE-5. The Teacher may update questions only in owned or authorized Study Sets and Question Banks.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The selected question is updated successfully. POST-2. The updated question information is displayed to the Teacher. POST-3. Existing study sessions, exam sessions, attempts, or reports that reference the question are handled according to integrity rules. POST-4. If the update fails or is cancelled, the original question data remains unchanged.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-41.0 Update Question** 1\. The Teacher opens an owned or authorized Study Set or Question Bank. 2\. The Teacher selects a question from the question list. 3\. The system displays the question detail page. 4\. The Teacher clicks Edit or Update Question. 5\. The system displays the Update Question form with existing question data. 6\. The Teacher updates question content, answer options, correct answer, score, explanation, tags, or chapter. 7\. The Teacher submits the updated question. 8\. The system validates the updated data and authorization for the target container. 9\. The system checks whether the update may affect active exams, completed attempts, learning records, or reports. 10\. The system saves the changes if allowed by integrity rules. 11\. The system displays a question saved success message (MSG29). 12\. The system displays the updated question detail page. |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-41.1 Cancel Update** 1\. At step 6 of the Normal Flow, the Teacher clicks Cancel. 2\. The system discards unsaved changes. 3\. The system returns the Teacher to the question detail page. 4\. The original question data remains unchanged. **UC-41.2 Update Metadata Only** 1\. At step 6 of the Normal Flow, the Teacher updates only metadata such as tags or chapter. 2\. The system validates that required question content and answer fields remain valid. 3\. The flow continues from step 8 of the Normal Flow. UC-41.3 Create New Version Instead of Direct Update 1\. At step 9 of the Normal Flow, the system detects that direct update may affect locked historical records. 2\. The system allows the Teacher to create a new version if supported. 3\. The original version remains preserved for historical records. 4\. The new version is saved for future use.                              |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-41.0.E1 Missing Required Data** 1\. At step 8 of the Normal Flow, the system detects missing required question data. 2\. The system displays a required information message (MSG02). 3\. The Teacher corrects the data. 4\. The flow continues from step 6 of the Normal Flow. **UC-41.0.E2 Invalid Updated Data** 1\. At step 8 of the Normal Flow, the system detects invalid question data. 2\. The system displays an invalid information message (MSG03). 3\. The Teacher corrects the data. 4\. The flow continues from step 6 of the Normal Flow.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | High. Teachers use this feature when correcting mistakes, improving question quality, or updating question metadata.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-07, BR-11, BR-12, BR-31, BR-32, BR-35                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |           |
| Other Information: | If the question has already been used in exams or completed practice sessions, the system should preserve historical attempt data according to reporting and audit rules.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The system can maintain question references safely when a question is updated.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |

#### **_2.4.10 Delete question_** {#2.4.10-delete-question}

| ID and Name:       | UC-42 Delete question                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Nguyễn Khắc Thành Sơn                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           | Date Created:     | 25/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Teacher                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         | Secondary Actors: |           |
| Description:       | As a Teacher, I want to delete, remove, hide, or archive a question from an authorized question container so that outdated or invalid content is no longer used.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The Teacher clicks the Delete, Remove, Hide, or Archive button on a question detail page or question list.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The user has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The user account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The selected question container exists. PRE-4. The selected question exists in the container. PRE-5. The user has delete or remove permission for the selected container.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The question is removed, hidden, archived, or deleted according to integrity rules. POST-2. The question is no longer available for new learning or authoring use in that container when removal is successful. POST-3. Historical learning, exam, and report data remain valid. POST-4. If the action fails or is cancelled, the question remains unchanged.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-42.0 Delete Question** 1\. The Teacher opens an owned or authorized Study Set or Question Bank. 2\. The Teacher selects a question from the question list. 3\. The Teacher clicks Delete, Remove, Hide, or Archive. 4\. The system displays a confirmation message. 5\. The Teacher confirms the action. 6\. The system validates Teacher permission and checks whether the question is referenced by practice sessions, exams, attempts, or reports. 7\. The system applies the allowed action according to integrity rules. 8\. The system displays a question status update success message (MSG29). 9\. The system displays the updated question list. |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-42.1 Cancel Deletion** 1\. At step 6 of the Normal Flow, the system detects that hard deletion may affect historical data. 2\. The system allows the Teacher to archive or hide the question if permitted. 3\. The Teacher confirms the archive or hide action. 4\. The system updates the question status and displays MSG29.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-42.0.E1 Unauthorized Question Container** 1\. At step 6 of the Normal Flow, the system detects that the Teacher does not have permission to delete, remove, hide, or archive the question. 2\. The system blocks the action and displays a permission error message (MSG11). 3\.
