The question remains unchanged.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |           |
| Priority:          | Medium                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | Medium. Teacher delete or remove questions when content becomes invalid, duplicated, or no longer useful.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-07, BR-11, BR-12, BR-31, BR-35                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| Other Information: | Deleting a copied Study Set question must not grant access to or modify the source Question Bank unless the Teacher explicitly manages that Question Bank.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The system can determine whether a question is allowed to be deleted based on its current usage status and related system rules.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |           |

#### **_2.4.11 Generate questions from material_** {#2.4.11-generate-questions-from-material}

| ID and Name:       | UC-43 Generate questions from material                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |            |
| :----------------- | :-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :--------- |
| Created By:        | Nguyễn Khắc Thành Sơn                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           | Date Created:     | 25/5/2026  |
| Primary Actor:     | Teacher                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         | Secondary Actors: | Gemini API |
| Description:       | As a Premium Teacher, I want to generate draft questions from uploaded learning material using AI so that I can quickly create questions for an authorized Study Set or Question Bank.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |            |
| Trigger:           | The Teacher clicks Generate Questions from Material from an owned or authorized Study Set or Question Bank.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |            |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Teacher has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The Teacher account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The active role is Teacher. PRE-4. The Teacher has active Premium access. PRE-5. The target Study Set or Question Bank exists. PRE-6. The Teacher has authoring permission for the target container. PRE-7. The uploaded or selected learning material is valid and readable by the system.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |            |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. AI-generated draft questions are displayed for review. POST-2. Approved valid questions are saved into the selected Study Set or Question Bank. POST-3. Unapproved or invalid generated questions are not saved. POST-4. If AI generation fails or is cancelled, no generated question is saved.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |            |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-43.0 Generate Questions from Material** 1\. The Teacher opens an owned or authorized Study Set or Question Bank. 2\. The Teacher clicks Generate Questions from Material. 3\. The system validates Premium access and target container authorization. 4\. The system displays the AI generation form. 5\. The Teacher uploads or selects learning material and chooses generation settings such as question type, number of questions, and question bank subject context. 6\. The Teacher submits the AI generation request. 7\. The system displays an AI processing message (MSG17). 8\. The system sends the request to Gemini API. 9\. Gemini API returns generated draft questions. 10\. The system displays generated draft questions in the preview step. 11\. The Teacher reviews, edits, removes, or approves generated drafts. 12\. The Teacher saves approved valid questions. 13\. The system saves approved questions into the selected container. 14\. The system displays a question saved success message (MSG29).                                                                                                                            |                   |            |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-43.1 Regenerate Questions** 1\. At step 11 of the Normal Flow, the Teacher chooses to regenerate draft questions. 2\. The system sends a new request to Gemini API using the selected material and settings. 3\. The flow continues from step 7 of the Normal Flow. **UC-43.2 Cancel AI Generation** 1\. At step 5 or step 11 of the Normal Flow, the Teacher cancels the process. 2\. The system discards unsaved generated drafts. 3\. No generated question is saved. **UC-43.3 Preview Required Before Saving** 1\. At step 12 of the Normal Flow, the Teacher attempts to save generated questions without completing preview. 2\. The system displays a preview required message (MSG31). 3\. The flow continues from step 10 of the Normal Flow.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |            |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-43.0.E1 Non-Premium Account** 1\. At step 3 of the Normal Flow, the system detects that the Teacher does not have active Premium access. 2\. The system blocks AI generation and displays a Premium-only feature message (MSG16). 3\. The use case ends. **UC-43.0.E2 Unauthorized Target Container** 1\. At step 3 of the Normal Flow, the system detects that the Teacher cannot save questions into the target container. 2\. The system blocks the action and displays a permission error message (MSG11). 3\. The use case ends. **UC-43.0.E3 Invalid Learning Material** 1\. At step 5 or step 6 of the Normal Flow, the system detects that the uploaded or selected material is missing, unreadable, or invalid. 2\. The system displays an invalid information message (MSG03). 3\. The Teacher corrects the material. 4\. The flow continues from step 5 of the Normal Flow. **UC-43.0.E4 Gemini API Failure** 1\. At step 8 or step 9 of the Normal Flow, Gemini API fails, times out, is rate-limited, or returns no usable content. 2\. The system displays an AI processing unavailable message (MSG18). 3\. No generated question is saved. |                   |            |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |            |
| Frequency of Use:  | High for Premium Teachers. Teachers use this feature to accelerate question creation from learning material.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |            |
| Business Rules:    | BR-07, BR-11, BR-12, BR-17, BR-31, BR-32, BR-34, BR-36, BR-37                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |            |
| Other Information: | AI-generated questions are drafts. The Teacher must review and approve them before saving.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |            |
| Assumptions:       | Gemini API can return structured draft questions that are editable before saving                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |            |

### **2.5 Study Set Creation and Learning** {#2.5-study-set-creation-and-learning}

#### **_2.5.1 View accessible study sets_** {#2.5.1-view-accessible-study-sets}

| ID and Name:       | UC-19 View accessible study sets                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Lê Hải Đăng                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               | Date Created:     | 20/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Learner, Teacher                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          | Secondary Actors: | None      |
| Description:       | As a Learner or Teacher, I want to view Study Sets that I am allowed to access so that I can study, manage, or use learning content according to my role and authorization.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The user opens the Accessible Study Sets page, dashboard study set area, class learning material page, or Study Sets menu.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The user has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The user account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The active role is Learner or Teacher. PRE-4. The system can determine Study Set accessibility based on visibility, ownership, authorization, or class assignment.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The system displays the list of Study Sets accessible to the user. POST-2. The user can select an accessible Study Set for supported actions. POST-3. No Study Set data is changed by viewing the list.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-19.0 View Accessible Study Sets** 1\. The user opens the Accessible Study Sets page. 2\. The system identifies the user’s active role. 3\. The system retrieves Study Sets accessible to the user. 4\. For a Learner, the system includes public Study Sets and Study Sets assigned through joined classes. 5\. For a Teacher, the system includes public Study Sets, owned Study Sets, and authorized Study Sets. 6\. The system filters out hidden, archived, deleted, restricted, or unauthorized Study Sets. 7\. The system displays the accessible Study Set list with relevant summary information. 8\. The user selects a Study Set. 9\. The system opens the selected Study Set detail page. |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-19.1 Search Or Filter Accessible Study Sets** 1\. At step 7, the user enters a keyword or selects filters such as subject, class, owner, or visibility. 2\. The system applies the search or filter condition. 3\. The system displays matching accessible Study Sets. **UC-19.2 No Accessible Study Sets Found** 1\. At step 3 or step 7, the system finds no accessible Study Sets. 2\. The system displays MSG45. 3\. The use case ends.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-19.0.E1 Unauthorized Access** 1\. At step 2 or step 6, the system detects that the user does not have permission to access the Study Set list or selected Study Set. 2\. The system blocks access and displays MSG11. **UC-19.0.E2 Study Set Not Available** 1\. At step 8, the selected Study Set is private, hidden, archived, deleted, restricted, or no longer assigned to the user. 2\. The system blocks access and displays MSG34. **UC-19.0.E3 Load Failure** 1\. At step 3, the system cannot load Study Set data. 2\. The system displays MSG13.                                                                                                                                           |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | High. Learners and Teachers access Study Sets frequently for learning and management.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-11, BR-12, BR-23                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Other Information: | Public search for Study Sets is handled by UC-02. This use case covers authenticated accessible Study Set lists.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The system can calculate Study Set accessibility based on public visibility, class assignment, ownership, and Teacher authorization.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |

#### **_2.5.2 Create study set_** {#2.5.2-create-study-set}

| ID and Name:       | UC-44 Create study set                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Lê Hải Đăng                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | Date Created:     | 20/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Teacher                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      | Secondary Actors: | None      |
| Description:       | As a Teacher, I want to create a Study Set so that I can organize learning content, add questions, and optionally assign the Study Set to classes.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The Teacher clicks Create Study Set from the Teacher dashboard, Study Sets page, or class learning material area.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Teacher has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The Teacher account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The active role is Teacher. PRE-4. The Teacher has permission to create Study Sets.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. A new Study Set is created successfully. POST-2. The new Study Set contains valid metadata. POST-3. The Teacher can add questions manually, import questions, generate questions from material, or copy questions from an authorized Question Bank where supported. POST-4. If the action fails or is cancelled, no Study Set is created.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-44.0 Create Study Set**1\. The Teacher opens the Create Study Set page. 2\. The system displays the Study Set creation form. 3\. The Teacher enters Study Set title, description, subject, visibility, and other required metadata. 4\. The Teacher submits the Study Set form. 5\. The system validates Teacher authorization and required Study Set information. 6\. The system creates the Study Set. 7\. The system displays MSG32. 8\. The system opens the Study Set detail or editor page. 9\. The Teacher may add questions through UC-37, UC-38, or UC-43. 10\. The Teacher may preview questions through UC-40 before saving them into the Study Set.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-44.1 Create Empty Study Set**1\. At step 9, the Teacher decides not to add questions immediately. 2\. The system keeps the Study Set saved as an empty Study Set. 3\. Learning modes remain unavailable until valid questions are added.**UC-44.2 Copy Questions From Authorized Question Bank** 1\. At step 9, the Teacher selects questions from an authorized Question Bank. 2\. The system validates Teacher authorization for the selected Question Bank. 3\. The Teacher previews the selected questions. 4\. The system copies selected question content into the Study Set. 5\. The copied questions become part of the Study Set. 6\. The system does not grant Learners direct access to the source Question Bank.**UC-44.3 Cancel Study Set Creation** 1\. At step 4, the Teacher cancels the action. 2\. The system discards unsaved Study Set information after confirmation. 3\. No Study Set is created. |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-44.0.E1 Missing Required Study Set Data** 1\. At step 5, the system detects missing required Study Set information. 2\. The system highlights missing fields and displays MSG02. 3\. The Teacher corrects the data. 4\. The flow continues from step 3\.**UC-44.0.E2 Invalid Study Set Data** 1\. At step 5, the system detects invalid Study Set information. 2\. The system highlights invalid fields and displays MSG03. 3\. The Teacher corrects the data. 4\. The flow continues from step 3\.**UC-44.0.E3 Unauthorized Creation** 1\. At step 5, the system detects that the Teacher is not authorized to create the Study Set. 2\. The system blocks the action and displays MSG11. **UC-44.2.E1 Unauthorized Question Bank** 1\. During UC-44.2, the system detects that the Teacher is not authorized to use the selected Question Bank. 2\. The system blocks the copy action and displays MSG11.             |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | High. Study Set creation is a core Teacher content management activity.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-11, BR-12, BR-23, BR-24, BR-31, BR-34                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |           |
| Other Information: | A Study Set is the primary learner-facing learning object. Question Banks are Teacher-managed repositories and are not directly exposed to Learners or Guests.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The system supports Study Sets without questions immediately after creation, but flashcard and quiz modes require available questions.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |

#### **_2.5.3 Assign study set to class_** {#2.5.3-assign-study-set-to-class}

| ID and Name:       | UC-45 Assign study set to class                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |               |
| :----------------- | :-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :------------ |
| Created By:        | Lê Hải Đăng                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   | Date Created:     | 20/5/2026     |
| Primary Actor:     | Teacher                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       | Secondary Actors: | Email Service |
| Description:       | As a Teacher, I want to assign an owned or authorized Study Set to a class or selected Learners so that Learners can access assigned learning content.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |               |
| Trigger:           | The Teacher clicks Assign to Class from a Study Set detail page or class learning material page.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |               |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Teacher has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The Teacher account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The active role is Teacher. PRE-4. The selected Study Set exists. PRE-5. The Teacher owns or is authorized to assign the selected Study Set. PRE-6. The target class exists and is managed by the Teacher.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |               |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The Study Set is assigned to the selected class or selected Learners. POST-2. Eligible Learners can access the assigned Study Set. POST-3. Assignment information is displayed in the class or Learner Study Set list. POST-4. Notifications are sent if notification is enabled.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |               |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-45.0 Assign Study Set To Class**1\. The Teacher opens an owned or authorized Study Set. 2\. The Teacher clicks Assign to Class. 3\. The system displays classes managed by the Teacher. 4\. The Teacher selects a target class. 5\. The Teacher confirms assignment settings. 6\. The system creates the Study Set assignment. 7\. The system notifies eligible Learners if notification is enabled. 8\. The system displays MSG33.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |               |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-45.1 Assign To Selected Learners**1\. At step 4, the Teacher selects individual Learners instead of the full class. 2\. The system validates that selected Learners belong to the managed class. 3\. The flow continues from step 5\.**UC-45.2 Cancel Assignment**1\. At step 5, the Teacher cancels assignment. 2\. The system discards assignment changes. 3\. No Study Set assignment is created. **UC-45.3 No Managed Class Available** 1\. At step 3, the system finds no class managed by the Teacher. 2\. The system displays MSG45. 3\. The use case ends.                                                                                                                       |                   |               |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-45.0.E1 Unauthorized Study Set**1\. At step 6, the system detects that the Teacher cannot assign the selected Study Set. 2\. The system blocks the action and displays MSG11.**UC-45.0.E2 Unauthorized Class**1\. At step 6, the system detects that the Teacher does not manage the selected class.2\. The system blocks the action and displays MSG11. **UC-45.0.E3 Study Set Not Available** 1\. At step 6, the selected Study Set is hidden, archived, deleted, restricted, or otherwise unavailable. 2\. The system blocks assignment and displays MSG34. **UC-45.0.E4 Load Failure** 1\. At step 3, the system cannot load class or Study Set data. 2\. The system displays MSG13. |                   |               |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |               |
| Frequency of Use:  | High. Teachers use this feature to distribute learning materials to classes.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |               |
| Business Rules:    | BR-11, BR-12, BR-18, BR-22, BR-23, BR-24, BR-34                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |               |
| Other Information: | Only Teachers can assign Study Sets to classes. Learners can access assigned Study Sets but cannot assign them.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |               |
| Assumptions:       | The system can determine Teacher management scope for classes and Study Sets.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |               |

#### **_2.5.4 Study flashcards_** {#2.5.4-study-flashcards}

| ID and Name:       | UC-05 Study flashcards                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Lê Hải Đăng                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         | Date Created:     | 19/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Guest, Learner                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      | Secondary Actors: | None      |
| Description:       | As a Guest or Learner, I want to study questions and answers using flashcard mode so that I can review learning content.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The user opens flashcard mode from a public Study Set or accessible Study Set detail page.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The selected Study Set exists. PRE-2. The selected Study Set contains at least one question. PRE-3. Guest access is allowed only when the Study Set is Public and not hidden. PRE-4. Authenticated Learners must have access to the selected Study Set.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The user completes or exits a flashcard study session. POST-2. For authenticated Learners, study progress may be saved. POST-3. Guests do not receive personal progress tracking unless they log in.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-05.0 Study Flashcards**1\. The user opens a public or accessible Study Set. 2\. The user clicks Study Flashcards. 3\. The system validates Study Set access. 4\. The system loads flashcards from Study Set questions. 5\. The system displays the first flashcard question. 6\. The user flips the flashcard to view the answer. 7\. The user marks the card or moves to the next flashcard. 8\. The system continues until the user completes the session or exits. 9\. The system saves progress for authenticated Learners. 10\. The system displays MSG12 when the session is completed.                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-05.1 Guest Studies Public Flashcards**1\. At step 3, the system detects that the user is Guest. 2\. The system allows flashcard mode only for Public Study Sets. 3\. The flow continues from step 4\.**UC-05.2 Shuffle Flashcards**1\. At step 4, the user selects shuffle mode if available.2\. The system randomizes flashcard order.3\. The flow continues from step 5\. **UC-05.3 Exit Flashcard Session** 1\. At step 7, the user exits flashcard mode before completing all cards. 2\. The system closes the flashcard session. 3\. For authenticated Learners, the system saves progress if supported.                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-05.0.E1 Unauthorized Study Set**1\. At step 3, the system detects that the user cannot access the selected Study Set.2\. The system blocks access and displays MSG11.**UC-05.0.E2 Study Set Not Available** 1\. At step 3, the selected Study Set is private, hidden, archived, deleted, restricted, or not assigned to the Learner. 2\. The system blocks access and displays MSG34.**UC-05.0.E3 No Flashcards Available** 1\. At step 4, the system detects that the Study Set has no available questions. 2\. The system displays MSG45 and does not start flashcard mode. **UC-05.0.E4 Load Failure** 1\. At step 4, the system cannot load flashcard data. 2\. The system displays MSG13. |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | High. Flashcard mode is a primary learning activity for public and accessible Study Sets.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-01, BR-02, BR-04, BR-23, BR-25                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |
| Other Information: | Flashcard mode uses Study Set questions. Question Banks are not directly studied by Learners or Guests.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The system can distinguish Guest public access from authenticated Learner Study Set access.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |           |

####

#### **_2.5.5 Take study set quiz_** {#2.5.5-take-study-set-quiz}

| ID and Name:       | UC-20 Take study set quiz                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Lê Hải Đăng                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | Date Created:     | 19/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Learner                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      | Secondary Actors: | None      |
| Description:       | As a Learner, I want to take a quiz generated from an accessible Study Set so that I can practice and assess my understanding.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The Learner clicks Take Quiz from an accessible Study Set detail page.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Learner has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The Learner account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The selected Study Set exists and is accessible to the Learner. PRE-4. The Study Set contains questions available for quiz mode.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The Learner’s quiz attempt is submitted. POST-2. The system records score, submitted answers, wrong answers, and learning progress. POST-3.
