The Learner can review wrong answers after quiz completion.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-20.0 Take Study Set Quiz** 1\. The Learner opens an accessible Study Set. 2\. The Learner clicks Take Quiz. 3\. The system validates Learner access to the Study Set. 4\. The system generates quiz questions from the Study Set. 5\. The Learner answers each question. 6\. The Learner submits the quiz. 7\. The system grades the quiz. 8\. The system saves quiz results, wrong answers, and learning progress. 9\. The system displays MSG14 with the quiz result summary. 10\. The Learner may proceed to UC-21 Review wrong answers.                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-20.1 Exit Before Submit** 1\. At step 5, the Learner exits quiz mode before submitting. 2\. The system handles unsaved answers according to configured quiz behavior. 3\. The quiz may be discarded or saved as incomplete if supported.**UC-20.2 Retake Quiz** 1\. After step 9, the Learner chooses to retake the quiz. 2\. The system generates a new quiz attempt from the accessible Study Set. 3\. The flow continues from step 5\.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-20.0.E1 Guest Attempts Quiz** 1\. At step 2 or step 3, the system detects that the user is Guest. 2\. The system blocks quiz mode and displays MSG11.**UC-20.0.E2 Unauthorized Study Set** 1\. At step 3, the system detects that the Learner cannot access the selected Study Set. 2\. The system blocks quiz mode and displays MSG11.**UC-20.0.E3 Study Set Not Available** 1\. At step 3, the selected Study Set is hidden, archived, deleted, restricted, or no longer assigned to the Learner. 2\. The system blocks quiz mode and displays MSG34. **UC-20.0.E4 No Questions Available** 1\. At step 4, the system detects that the Study Set has no questions available for quiz mode. 2\. The system displays MSG45 and does not start the quiz. |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | High. Learners use quiz mode frequently to practice Study Sets.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-04, BR-11, BR-12, BR-23, BR-26                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| Other Information: | Quiz mode is available only to authenticated Learners.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The system can generate quiz questions from Study Set questions without exposing any source Question Bank.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |

#### **_2.5.6 Review wrong answers_** {#2.5.6-review-wrong-answers}

| ID and Name:       | UC-21 Review wrong answers                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Lê Hải Đăng                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   | Date Created:     | 19/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Learner                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       | Secondary Actors: | None      |
| Description:       | As a Learner, I want to review and retry questions that I answered incorrectly so that I can improve weak areas after completing quiz mode.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The Learner clicks Review Wrong Answers from the quiz result page, learning progress page, or wrong-answer review page.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Learner has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The Learner account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The Learner has completed at least one quiz attempt. PRE-4. The system has recorded wrong answers for the Learner.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The Learner views their own wrong-answer list. POST-2. The Learner may retry wrong questions. POST-3. The system updates learning progress if the Learner retries questions.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-21.0 Review Wrong Answers** 1\. The Learner opens the quiz result page or wrong-answer review page. 2\. The Learner clicks Review Wrong Answers. 3\. The system retrieves wrong answers from the Learner’s completed quiz attempts. 4\. The system displays the wrong-answer list with question content, selected answer, correct answer, and explanation if available. 5\. The Learner reviews the wrong answers. 6\. The Learner selects a wrong question to retry. 7\. The system displays the selected question for retry. 8\. The Learner submits a new answer. 9\. The system checks the answer and updates learning progress. 10 . The system displays the updated review result. |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-21.1 No Wrong Answers** 1\. At step 3, the system finds no wrong answers for the Learner. 2\. The system displays MSG15. 3\. The use case ends.**UC-21.2 Review Without Retry** 1\. At step 5, the Learner reviews wrong answers without retrying them. 2\. The system keeps the wrong-answer history unchanged. 3\. The Learner exits the review page.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-21.0.E1 Unauthorized Wrong-Answer Access** 1\. At step 3, the system detects that the Learner is attempting to access another user’s wrong-answer data. 2\. The system blocks access and displays MSG11.**UC-21.0.E2 Study Set Not Available** 1\. At step 4, the related Study Set is no longer available to the Learner. 2\. The system displays MSG34 and does not expose restricted content.**UC-21.0.E3 Failed To Load Wrong Answers** 1\. At step 3, the system cannot load wrong-answer data. 2\. The system displays MSG13.                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | High. Learners review mistakes frequently after practice quizzes.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-11, BR-12, BR-23, BR-26, BR-27                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |           |
| Other Information: | Wrong-answer review must display only the current Learner’s own quiz history and mistakes.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The system records quiz attempts, selected answers, correct answers, and wrong-answer data during UC-20.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |

#### **_2.5.7 Request AI answer explanation_** {#2.5.7-request-ai-answer-explanation}

| ID and Name:       | UC-22 Request AI answer explanation                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |            |
| :----------------- | :--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :--------- |
| Created By:        | Lê Hải Đăng                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              | Date Created:     | 19/5/2026  |
| Primary Actor:     | Learner                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | Secondary Actors: | Gemini API |
| Description:       | As a Learner, I want to request an AI-generated explanation for a question and answer so that I can understand why an answer is correct or incorrect.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |            |
| Trigger:           | The Learner clicks Request AI Explanation from the quiz result page, wrong-answer review page, or question detail area.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |            |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Learner has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The Learner account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The Learner has active Premium access. PRE-4. The selected question exists. PRE-5. The Learner is authorized to view the selected question and answer. PRE-6. Gemini API is available.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |            |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The system displays an AI-generated explanation for the selected question and answer.POST-2. The explanation may be stored in the Learner’s learning history if supported.POST-3. If the AI request fails, no learning answer data is changed.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |            |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-22.0 Request AI Answer Explanation** 1\. The Learner opens a quiz result, wrong-answer review, or question detail page. 2\. The Learner clicks Request AI Explanation. 3\. The system validates Learner authorization for the question. 4\. The system checks the Learner’s Premium status. 5\. The system displays MSG17 while processing the request. 6\. The system sends the question, answer, and learning context to Gemini API. 7\. Gemini API generates an explanation. 8\. The system receives and validates the generated explanation. 9\. The system displays the AI-generated explanation to the Learner.                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |            |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-22.1 Request Explanation For Correct Answer** 1\. At step 2, the Learner requests an explanation for a correctly answered question. 2\. The system continues the same validation and AI request process. 3\. The flow continues from step 3\. **UC-22.2 Request Explanation From Wrong-Answer Review** 1\. At step 2, the Learner requests explanation from a wrong-answer review item. 2\. The system uses the wrong answer, correct answer, and question context in the AI request. 3\. The flow continues from step 3\.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |            |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-22.0.E1 Non-Premium Learner** 1\. At step 4, the system detects that the Learner does not have active Premium access. 2\. The system blocks the AI feature and displays MSG16. **UC-22.0.E2 Unauthorized Question** 1\. At step 3, the system detects that the Learner is not authorized to view the selected question or answer. 2\. The system blocks the request and displays MSG11. **UC-22.0.E3 Study Set Not Available** 1\. At step 3, the related Study Set is private, hidden, archived, deleted, restricted, or no longer assigned to the Learner. 2\. The system blocks the request and displays MSG34. **UC-22.0.E4 AI Service Failure** 1\. At step 6 or step 7, Gemini API is unavailable, rate-limited, times out, or returns no usable content. 2\. The system displays MSG18. 3\. The Learner may try again later. |                   |            |
| Priority:          | Medium                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |            |
| Frequency of Use:  | Medium. Learners use AI explanations mainly when they need help understanding difficult questions.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |            |
| Business Rules:    | BR-11, BR-12, BR-17, BR-23, BR-27, BR-36, BR-37                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |            |
| Other Information: | AI-generated explanations are support content and should not replace the official correct answer stored in the system.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |            |
| Assumptions:       | The system can send only necessary question and answer context to Gemini API.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |            |

####

### **2.6 Exam Session** {#2.6-exam-session}

#### **_2.6.1 View available exams_** {#2.6.1-view-available-exams}

| ID and Name:       | UC-24 View available exams                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Vương Trung Quốc                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        | Date Created:     | 19/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Learner                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 | Secondary Actors: |           |
| Description:       | As a Learner, I want to view available exams so that I can know which exam sessions I am allowed to take.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The learner logs into the system and navigates to the exam section.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The learner is successfully logged into the system. PRE-2. The learner is a member of at least one class. PRE-3. Teachers have created and published exam sessions for those classes.                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The system successfully retrieves and displays the filtered list of exam sessions. POST-2. The learner can identify which exams are currently open for attempts.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **24.0 View available exams** 1\. The learner navigates to the exam section. 2\. The system identifies the classes the learner belongs to. 3\. The system filters for all published exam sessions associated with those classes based on their visibility settings and current timestamps. 4\. The system displays the list of exams. 5\. The learner views the exam sessions and their current states. |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **24.1 Filter and Search Exams** 1\. The learner enters a keyword in the search bar or selects a specific filter. 2\. The system updates the list to display only exams matching the search criteria (MSG45). 3\. The learner views the filtered results. **24.1. No exams found** 1\. The system finds no published exams for the learner’s classes. 2\. The system displays a message.                |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **24.0. E1 Failed to load exam list** 1\. A database connection error occurs while retrieving exam data. 2\. The system displays a "Retry" button or an error notification (MSG13). 3\. The learner attempts to refresh the page.                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | Learners use this daily or weekly to check for assigned assessments and scheduled exams.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-01, BR-07, BR-09, BR-38                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |           |
| Other Information: | The dashboard may use color-coding to help learners quickly distinguish the urgency of each session.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The SQP System efficiently handles real-time status updates so that an exam automatically changes the exam’s status as soon as the start time is reached without requiring a page hard-refresh.                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |           |

#### **_2.6.2 View available exam information_** {#2.6.2-view-available-exam-information}

| ID and Name:       | UC-25 View available exam information                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Vương Trung Quốc                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           | Date Created:     | 19/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Learner                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    | Secondary Actors: |           |
| Description:       | As a Learner, I want to view exam information before starting an exam so that I can understand the exam time, duration, attempt limit, and result visibility rules.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The learner clicks on a specific exam card or clicks an exam invitation link from their email.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The learner is successfully logged into the system. PRE-2. The learner has permission to access the exam.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The learner clearly understands the exam rules and conditions. POST-2. If eligible, the learner is presented with the option to start the exam.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **25.0 View Exam Information** 1.The learner selects a specific exam to view its details. 2\. The system retrieves the exam session configuration and the learner's attempt history from the database. 3\. The system validates the current server time against the exam's time window and checks the learner's remaining attempts. 4\. Based on the validation, the system displays the exam information page and enables the start button if eligible. . |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **25.1 Exam Not Yet Started** 1\. The system determines the current server time is before the exam's Start Time. 2\. The system displays all exam information but disables the start button. 3\. The system displays a countdown timer. 4\. Once the countdown reaches zero, the system automatically enables the start button.                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **25.0. E1 Exam Session Unavailable or Deleted** 1\. The system cannot find the exam session. 2\. The system displays an error message (MSG38). 3\. The system provides a button to return to the Dashboard.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | Every time a learner intends to take an exam or check upcoming exam schedules.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-07, BR-11, BR-12, BR-38                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |           |
| Other Information: | In this page, learners can prepare themselves mentally and check their internet connection before clicking Start, reducing accidental exam entries.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The UI clearly differentiates between general class assignments and high-stakes real-time exams using distinct icons or tags.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |           |

#### **_2.6.3 Take exam_** {#2.6.3-take-exam}

| ID and Name:       | UC-26 Take exam                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Vương Trung Quốc                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            | Date Created:     | 19/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Learner                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     | Secondary Actors: |           |
| Description:       | As a Learner, I want to take a real-time exam so that I can complete the assigned assessment under the configured exam rules.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The user selects an active exam session from their dashboards or clicks the invitation link.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The learner is successfully logged into the system. PRE-2. The exam session is published and within the start and end time window. PRE-3. The learner belongs to the class assigned to the exam session. PRE-4. The learner has not exceeded the maximum allowed attempts for this exam.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The learner’s exam attempt is locked and saved in the database. POST-2. The system calculates and stores the final score and statistics. POST-3. The system updates the class and exam session statistics. POST-4. The learner cannot modify their answers for this attempt.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **26.0 Take Real-time exam** 1.The learner navigates to the dashboard and selects an active exam session. 2\. The system validates the learner’s eligibility. 3\. The system generates an exam attempt and displays the exam interface, including questions, options, and a countdown timer. 4\. The learner reads the question and selects an answer. 5\. The system automatically saves the selected answer in real-time. 6\. The learner navigates through the questions and answers them. 7\. The learner clicks the “Submit” button. 8\. The system prompts the learner to confirm the submission. 9\. The learner confirms. 10\. The system locks the attempt, collects all answers, and auto-grades the exam. 11\. The system displays the completion status (MSG39) and results based on the teacher’s visibility settings.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **26.1 Time Expires (Auto-submit)** 1\. The countdown timer reaches zero while the learner is still taking the exam. 2\. The system automatically forces the submission of the exam. 3\. The system locks the attempt and auto-grades the saved answers. 4\. The system notifies the learner that the time is up and displays the screen based on the teacher’s configuration(MSG40). **26.2 Page Reload or Browser Close** 1\. The learner accidentally reloads the page or closes the browser tab during the exam. 2\. The learner logs back in and re-enters the exam session. 3\. The system restores the latest auto-saved state and resumes the countdown timer without resetting the time. 4\. The learner continues the exam from where they left off. **26.3 Network Disconnect & Reconnect** 1\. The learner loses internet connection during the exam. 2\. The system displays a network warning but caches the learner's new answers locally. 3\. The internet connection is restored. 4\. The system automatically syncs the cached answers to the server and confirms the save state (MSG33). |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **26.0. E1 Learner Not Eligible** 1\. The system determines the learner is not in the class, the exam has expired, or the maximum attempts have been reached. 2\. The system displays an access denied message (MSG38 for permission/attempts errors). 3\. The use case ends without generating an exam attempt. **26.1. E2 Submission Failure (Network Down)** 1\. The learner clicks "Submit", but the network is disconnected. 2\. The system displays an error message indicating the submission cannot be processed (MSG13). 3\. The system continuously retries syncing in the background until the connection is restored to finalize the submission.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | Learners frequently use this feature during exams conducted by teachers.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-07, BR-11, BR-12, BR-38, BR-40                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |           |
| Other Information: | Learner progress is synced by the system during the exam for recovery purposes only.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | \- The teacher has successfully configured and published the exam session with valid question banks. \- The system has sufficient server resources to handle concurrent auto-save requests from multiple learners during a large-scale exam.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |           |

####

#### **_2.6.4 View exam result_** {#2.6.4-view-exam-result}

| ID and Name:       | UC-27 View exam result                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Vương Trung Quốc                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | Date Created:     | 19/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Learner                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         | Secondary Actors: |           |
| Description:       | As a Learner, I want to view my exam result when it is available so that I can understand my score and performance after submission.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The learner clicks the "View Result" button immediately after submitting an exam or selects a completed exam from their Exam History                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The learner is successfully logged into the system. PRE-2. The learner has submitted the exam attempt. PRE-3. The system has completed the auto-grading process for that attempt.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The learner views their performance feedback according to the permitted visibility level.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **27.0 View Exam Score** 1\. The learner requests to view the result of a completed exam by clicking the view result button. 2\. The system retrieves the exam session's configuration rules and the learner's graded attempt from the database. 3\. The system checks the configuration by the teacher. 4\. The system retrieves the total score and percentage. 5\. The system displays the final score to the learner when the visibility rule allows scores. 6\. The learner reviews their score and exits the page. |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **27.1 View Completion Status Only (Score Hidden)** 1\. In Step 3 of the Normal Flow, the system determines the visibility rule is set to hide score (MSG41). 2\. The system displays a successfully submitted message. 3\. The learner views the completion status and exits the page. **27.2 View Question Answer Review** 1\. In Step 3 of the Normal Flow, the system determines the visibility rule is set to question-answer review. 2\. The system displays the score plus each question, the learner's selected answer, and the correct answer. 3\. The learner reviews the detailed result and exits the page. |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **27.0. E1 Failed to Retrieve Result Data** 1\. The system encounters a database or network error while trying to fetch the graded attempt. 2\. The system displays an error message (MSG13). 3\. The learner may click a button to retry or return to the dashboard.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | After every submitted real-time exam and whenever learners review their past performance.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-07, BR-11, BR-12, BR-40                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |
| Other Information: | By completely restricting access to the detailed answer keys, the system ensures exam integrity and prevents questions from being leaked while other learners might still be taking the test.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | Auto-grading is instantaneous upon submission, ensuring that the score or completion status is ready the exact moment the learner requests to view it.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |           |
