#### **_2.6.5 Create exam session_** {#2.6.5-create-exam-session}

| ID and Name:       | UC-46 Create exam session                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |               |
| :----------------- | :---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :------------ |
| Created By:        | Vương Trung Quốc                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            | Date Created:     | 23/5/2026     |
| Primary Actor:     | Teacher                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     | Secondary Actors: | Email Service |
| Description:       | As a Teacher, I want to create an official exam session for a class so that Learners can take a structured assessment.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |               |
| Trigger:           | The Teacher navigates to a specific class dashboard and creates exam sessions.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |               |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Teacher is successfully logged into the system. PRE-2. The Teacher manages at least one active class. PRE-3. The Teacher has access to at least one valid question bank containing questions.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |               |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The new exam session is successfully created and saved in the system database. POST-2. The system generates a unique access code or invitation link for the exam session. POST-3. A notification is triggered and sent to all learners within the assigned class. POST-4. The exam session appears in the upcoming schedules for both the Teacher and the Learners.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |               |
| Normal Flow:       | **46.0 Create Exam Session** 1\. The Teacher selects a specific class and initiates the "Create Exam Session" function. 2\. The Teacher selects one or multiple question banks to draw questions from. 3\. The Teacher configures the exam session. 4\. The Teacher submits the exam configuration. 5\. The system validates the configuration, verifying that the selected question banks contain enough valid questions to satisfy the configured total. 6\. The system creates the exam session, generates the access code/link, and saves the data. 7\. The Notification Service sends an automated alert to the learners in the class. 8\. The system redirects the Teacher to the class dashboard, displaying the newly created exam session (MSG35). |                   |               |
| Alternative Flows: | **46.1 Save Exam as Draft** 1\. In Step 4, the Teacher clicks "Save as Draft" instead of "Submit/Publish". 2\. The system skips the validation for complete configuration and saves the current progress. 3\. The system does not generate notifications or access links. 4\. The exam session is saved with a "Draft" status for future editing.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |               |
| Exceptions:        | **46.0. E1 Insufficient Questions** 1\. In Step 5, the system detects that the required number of questions exceeds the available questions in the selected banks. 2\. The system halts the creation process and displays a specific warning message (MSG37). 3\. The Teacher adjusts the configuration or selects additional question banks. **46.0. E2 Invalid Time Window** 1\. The system determines that the Start Time is in the past, or the End Time is earlier than the Start Time. 2\. The system highlights the time input fields and displays a validation error (MSG37). 3\. The Teacher corrects the time configuration.                                                                                                                      |                   |               |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |               |
| Frequency of Use:  | Medium. Used whenever a Teacher needs to conduct a formal assessment, midterm, or final exam for a class.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |               |
| Business Rules:    | BR-07, BR-11, BR-12, BR-38, BR-39                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |               |
| Other Information: | The UI provides real-time calculation of available questions as the Teacher selects different question banks to prevent the "Insufficient Questions" exception.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |               |
| Assumptions:       | The system automatically controls the exam session's availability strictly based on the configured Start and End times.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |               |

#### **_2.6.6 Configure exam settings_** {#2.6.6-configure-exam-settings}

| ID and Name:       | UC-47 Configure exam settings                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Vương Trung Quốc                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       | Date Created:     | 23/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Teacher                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | Secondary Actors: |           |
| Description:       | As a Teacher, I want to configure exam settings so that exam time, attempts, randomization, and result visibility follow the intended assessment rules.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The Teacher selects an existing exam session from the class dashboard and clicks the button for configuration.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Teacher is successfully logged into the system. PRE-2. The target exam session exists in the system. PRE-3. The Teacher is authorized to manage the class associated with this exam.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The system successfully updates and saves the new configuration in the database. POST-2. The exam session behavior adapts to the newly applied settings.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **47.0 Configure Exam Settings** 1\. The Teacher accesses the configuration interface of the selected exam session. 2\. The Teacher inputs or modifies the exam parameters and clicks save. 3\. The system validates the input data. 4\. The system saves the updated configuration and displays a success confirmation to the Teacher (MSG36).                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **47.1 Discard Changes** 1\. During configuration, the Teacher clicks the button for cancel and discard. 2\. The system ignores all unsaved inputs. 3\. The system redirects the Teacher back to the previous dashboard.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **47.0. E1 Invalid Time Window** 1\. The system determines that the End Time is configured earlier than the Start Time. 2\. The system blocks the save action and highlights the error fields (MSG37). 3\. The Teacher corrects the timeline and resubmits. **47.0. E2 Exam Already Active** 1\. The Teacher attempts to modify critical settings of an exam session that is currently running or has already concluded. 2\. The system prevents the changes to maintain exam integrity and displays a warning message (MSG11). 3\. The use case ends. |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | Medium. Teachers use this feature to finalize draft exams or adjust schedules before the exam starts.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-07, BR-11, BR-12, BR-38, BR-39                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |
| Other Information: | To ensure a smooth user experience, the interface should utilize standard UI components like date-time pickers, toggle switches for randomization, and dropdowns for visibility settings to minimize manual input errors.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The system distinguishes between exam states to strictly control which configuration fields remain editable.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |           |

The system renders the exam information page, displaying all retrieved details clearly.                                                                              |                   |           |

### **2.7 Analytics & Reporting** {#2.7-analytics-&-reporting}

#### **_2.7.1 View personal learning progress_** {#2.7.1-view-personal-learning-progress}

| ID and Name:       | UC-23 View personal learning progress                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Lê Hải Đăng                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        | Date Created:     | 22/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Learner                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            | Secondary Actors: |           |
| Description:       | As a Learner, I want to view my personal learning progress so that I can track practiced questions, accuracy, repeated mistakes, and weak subjects.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The Learner clicks the “Learning Progress”, “Progress”, “Analytics”, or “My Performance” option from the dashboard, study set page, quiz result page, or learning history page.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Learner has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The Learner account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The Learner has permission to access personal learning analytics. PRE-4. The system has learning activity data from at least one flashcard session, quiz attempt, wrong-answer review, or study set activity. PRE-5. The learning progress module is available.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The system displays the Learner’s personal learning progress summary. POST-2. The Learner can view practiced questions, accuracy rate, completed study sets, repeated mistakes, and weak subjects. POST-3. The Learner can identify areas that need further practice. POST-4. No learning data is changed unless the Learner starts another learning activity from the progress page.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-23.0 View Personal Learning Progress** 1\. The Learner opens the “Learning Progress” page. 2\. The system retrieves the Learner’s flashcard sessions, quiz attempts, wrong-answer records, and study set activity history. 3\. The system calculates learning indicators such as practiced questions, accuracy rate, completed study sets, repeated mistakes, weak subjects, and recent activity. 4\. The system displays the personal learning progress dashboard. 5\. The Learner reviews the summary statistics. 6\. The Learner selects a specific study set, subject, or class to view detailed progress. 7\. The system displays detailed progress information for the selected scope. 8\. The Learner may choose to continue studying, retry wrong questions, or open a related study set. |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-23.1 Filter Learning Progress** 1\. The Learner selects filters such as class, study set, subject, date range, or activity type. 2\. The system applies the selected filters. 3\. The system recalculates progress indicators based on the selected scope. 4\. The system displays the filtered progress results. **UC-23.2 No Learning Activity Data** 1\. The system finds that the Learner has no learning activity data. 2\. The system displays an empty state message. 3\. The system suggests starting a study set, flashcard session, or quiz.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-23.0. E1 Learning Data Not Found** 1\. The system cannot find learning data for the Learner. 2\. The system displays an empty progress message. 3\. The use case ends or allows the Learner to start a learning activity. **UC-23.0. E2 Failed to Load Progress Data** 1\. The system fails to retrieve or calculate progress data due to a system or network error. 2\. The system displays an error message. **UC-23.0. E3 Invalid Filter Criteria** 1\. The Learner selects invalid or conflicting filter criteria. 2\. The system displays a validation message.                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | High. Learners use this feature regularly to monitor learning outcomes, identify weak areas, and decide what to practice next.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-01, BR-03, BR-07, BR-09, BR-24                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Other Information: | Learning progress should be generated from actual study activities, quiz attempts, wrong-answer review, and study set completion records.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The system accurately records learning activities and can calculate progress indicators from stored learning data.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |           |

#### **_2.7.2 View learning analytics_** {#2.7.2-view-learning-analytics}

| ID and Name:       | UC-49 View learning analytics                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Phạm Minh Hải                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | Date Created:     | 25/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Teacher                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        | Secondary Actors: | None      |
| Description:       | As a Teacher, I want to view learning analytics so that I can evaluate learner performance, class progress, question quality, and exam outcomes.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The Teacher clicks on the "Analytics", "Reports", or "Class Performance" menu options from the teacher dashboard.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Teacher has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The Teacher account is active. PRE-3. The Analytics & Reporting module is online and fully synchronized with the examination database.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The system displays real-time visual charts, accuracy trends, and metric summaries. POST-2.No learner score, answer log, or profile data is modified by this use case.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-49.0 View Learning Analytics** 1\. The Teacher opens the "Analytics" dashboard. 2\. The system gets the grade data from the database for all of the teacher's classes. 3\. The system shows a summary page with the main statistics: average scores, how fast learners finished exams, top-performing learners, and subjects where learners struggle. 4\. The Teacher clicks on a specific class or exam to see more details. 5\. The system loads the detailed information and displays it in tabs such as learner rankings and question performance reports. 6\. The Teacher reviews the charts and data.                                                                                                |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-49.1 Filter Analytics by Category or Timeframe** 1\. The Teacher selects a specific filter, such as a date range, a learner group, or a subject subject tag. 2\. The system applies the search or filter criteria. 3\. The system updates the graphs and charts to match the chosen filter. **UC-49.2 No Analytics Available (New Class State)** 1\. The system detects that the chosen class or exam has no completed submissions or recorded answer logs. 2\. The system displays a message indicating "No analytical data recorded yet." 3\. The system provides quick links to assign a study set or activate an exam session.                                                                          |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-49.0. E1 Session Expired** 1\. The system determines that the Teacher’s authorization session token has expired. 2\. The system saves the target state redirect route and drops the user back to the primary Login page with an alert message. 3\. The use case ends. **UC-49.0. E2 High-Volume Data Compilation Timeout** 1\. The system attempts to aggregate historical performance data across too many massive tracking arrays simultaneously, causing a database query execution timeout. 2\. The system halts the pipeline cleanly and generates an alert notification: "Data collection timed out due to high volume. Please narrow down your target class or date range." 3\. The use case ends. |                   |           |
| Priority:          | Medium                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | Medium to High. Teachers monitor progress after assignments and exams.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-07, BR-11, BR-12, BR-18, BR-27, BR-40                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Other Information: | Charts should be optimized for clear visual interpretation, using standard color codes (e.g., green for high accuracy, red for weak subjects).                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The analytics compilation engines accurately reflect backend exam logs without omitting valid submissions.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |           |

#### **_2.7.3 Export report_** {#2.7.3-export-report}

| ID and Name:       | UC-50 Export report                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Phạm Minh Hải                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            | Date Created:     | 25/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Teacher                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | Secondary Actors: | None      |
| Description:       | As a Teacher, I want to export scoreboards or analytics reports so that I can store, share, or analyze learning and exam results outside the platform.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The Teacher clicks the "Export Report", "Download CSV", or "Save as PDF" button located inside any analytics dashboard, or class list page.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Teacher is authenticated and active. PRE-2. The Teacher is viewing analytics or scoreboard data. PRE-3. The Teacher is authorized for the selected class, exam, Study Set, or Learner scope.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. A report file is generated in the selected format. POST-2. The browser receives the file for download. POST-3. Export action may be logged.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-50.0 Export Report** 1\. The Teacher clicks Export on an analytics or grade page. 2\. The system displays export configuration such as format, scope, and summary/detailed option. 3\. The Teacher selects Excel, CSV, or PDF and confirms. 4\. The system validates authorization and active data scope. 5\. The system retrieves the latest data and generates the file. 6\. The system triggers browser download. 7\. The system displays MSG44. |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-50.1 Cancel Export** 1\. The Teacher closes or cancels export configuration. 2\. The system returns to the analytics page without generating a file.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-50.0.E1 File Generation Error** 1\. The system fails to serialize or generate the file. 2\. The system displays MSG13. 3\. The use case ends. **UC-50.0.E2 No Matching Data** 1\. The selected filters produce no exportable records. 2\. The system displays MSG45. **UC-50.0.E3 Unauthorized Export Scope** 1\. The Teacher selects data outside authorized scope. 2\. The system displays MSG11.                                                 |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | Medium. Used heavily during reporting periods.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-07, BR-11, BR-12, BR-18, BR-40                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |           |
| Other Information: | Exported reports should include clear headers and selected filter context.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The client browser permits file downloads.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |

### **2.8 Payment & Subscription** {#2.8-payment-&-subscription}

#### **_2.8.1 View premium plans_** {#2.8.1-view-premium-plans}

| ID and Name:       | UC-06 View premium plans                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Nguyễn Khắc Thành Sơn                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | Date Created:     | 25/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Guest, Learner, Teacher                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | Secondary Actors: |           |
| Description:       | As a Guest, Learner, or Teacher, I want to view available Premium plans so that I can compare their benefits before deciding whether to upgrade.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The user clicks the “Premium Plans”, “Upgrade”, or “View Plans” option from the homepage, dashboard, profile page, or feature limitation message.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The platform is online and accessible. PRE-2. Premium plan data has been configured and is available in the system. PRE-3. The user has access to the page or screen where Premium plans can be viewed.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The system displays available Premium plans and related benefit information. POST-2. If the user is authenticated, the system allows the user to continue to the upgrade process. POST-3. No payment transaction is created until the user selects a plan and proceeds to payment.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-06.0 View premium plans** 1\. The user opens the Premium Plans page. 2\. The system retrieves the list of active Premium plans. 3\. The system displays plan information, including plan name, price, billing period, available features, limitations, and Premium benefits. 4\. The user reviews and compares the available plans. 5\. The user selects a plan to view more details. 6\. The system displays detailed benefits and conditions of the selected plan. 7\. If the user is an authenticated Learner or Teacher, the system allows the user to continue to UC-16 Upgrade to Premium. 8\. If the user is a Guest, the system displays login or registration options before upgrade.                    |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-06.3 User Already Has Active Premium** 1\. The authenticated user opens the Premium Plans page while already having an active Premium subscription. 2\. The system displays the current Premium status, active plan, and expiration date. 3\. The system may allow the user to renew, extend, or view subscription details depending on business rules.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-06.0. E1 No Active Premium Plans Available** 1\. The system cannot find any active Premium plans. 2\. The system displays a no matching data message (MSG45). 3\. The use case ends. **UC-06.0. E2 Plan Data Retrieval Failed** 1\. The system fails to retrieve Premium plan data due to a database or network error. 2\. The system displays a data loading failure message (MSG13). 3\. The use case ends. **UC-06.0. E3 Selected Plan No Longer Available** 1\. The user selects a plan that has just been disabled or removed by the system. 2\. The system displays an invalid information message (MSG03). 3\. The system refreshes the Premium plan list. 4\. The user may select another available plan. |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | Medium to High. Guests may view plans before registration, while Learners and Teachers may view plans when they need Premium features such as AI explanation or AI question generation.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-01, BR-15, BR-17                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |           |
| Other Information: | Premium plan information should clearly show which features are unlocked for Learners and Teachers. The page should also explain payment conditions, subscription duration, and any renewal or expiration rules if supported.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The system maintains accurate Premium plan configuration, including price, duration, feature limits, and availability status.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |           |

####

#### **_2.8.2 Upgrade to Premium_** {#2.8.2-upgrade-to-premium}

| ID and Name:       | UC-16 Upgrade to Premium                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |                                |
| :----------------- | :--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :----------------------------- |
| Created By:        | Nguyễn Khắc Thành Sơn                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | Date Created:     | 25/5/2026                      |
| Primary Actor:     | Learner, Teacher                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     | Secondary Actors: | Payment Gateway, Email Service |
| Description:       | As a Learner or Teacher, I want to upgrade to a Premium plan so that I can access Premium features after successful payment.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |                                |
| Trigger:           | The authenticated Learner or Teacher clicks the “Upgrade”, “Buy Premium”, or “Continue to Payment” button after selecting a Premium plan.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |                                |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The user has logged in successfully as a Learner or Teacher. PRE-2. The selected Premium plan exists and is active. PRE-3. The user’s account is active and not locked. PRE-4. The Payment Gateway is available for processing payment. PRE-5.
