The user has not already completed the same active payment transaction.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                   |                                |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. If payment is successful, the system activates Premium access for the user. POST-2. The system records the payment transaction and subscription information. POST-3. The system updates the user’s Premium status and expiration date according to the selected plan. POST-4. The system sends or displays a successful upgrade notification. POST-5. If payment fails or is cancelled, Premium access is not activated and the user can retry or choose another payment method.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |                                |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-16.0 Upgrade to Premium** 1\. The authenticated Learner or Teacher selects an active Premium plan. 2\. The system displays the selected plan summary, including price, duration, and Premium benefits. 3\. The user confirms the selected plan. 4\. The system displays available payment methods. 5\. The user chooses a payment method. 6\. The system creates a pending payment transaction. 7\. The system redirects or sends the payment request to the Payment Gateway. 8\. The user completes payment through the Payment Gateway. 9\. The Payment Gateway returns a successful payment confirmation to the system. 10\. The system validates the payment confirmation. 11\. The system activates Premium access for the user. 12\. The system records the transaction and subscription details. 13\. The system displays a payment success message. 14\. The system requests the notification service to send an upgrade success notification to the user. 15\. The user can access Premium features based on their role.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |                                |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-16.1 User Chooses Another Payment Method** 1\. At step 5 of the Normal Flow, the user decides to use a different payment method. 2\. The system displays the available payment methods again. 3\. The user selects another payment method. 4\. The flow continues from step 6 of the Normal Flow. **UC-16.2 Payment Fails and User Retries** 1\. At step 9 of the Normal Flow, the Payment Gateway returns a failed payment result. 2\. The system records the transaction as failed. 3\. The system displays a payment not completed message (MSG43). 4\. The user chooses to retry payment or choose another payment method. 5\. The flow continues from step 4 of the Normal Flow. **UC-16.3 User Cancels Payment** 1\. At step 8 of the Normal Flow, the user cancels payment on the Payment Gateway page. 2\. The Payment Gateway returns a cancelled payment result to the system. 3\. The system records the transaction as cancelled. 4\. The system does not activate Premium access. 5\. The system displays MSG43. 6\. The system returns the user to the upgrade page and allows another attempt. **UC-16.4 User Already Has Active Premium** 1\. At step 1 of the Normal Flow, the system detects that the user already has active Premium access. 2\. The system displays the current Premium plan and expiration date. 3\. The user may cancel, renew, or extend the subscription depending on supported business rules.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |                                |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-16.0. E1 Selected Plan Invalid or Inactive** 1\. At step 1 or step 3 of the Normal Flow, the system detects that the selected Premium plan does not exist or is no longer active. 2\. The system displays an invalid information message (MSG03). 3\. The system redirects the user to the Premium Plans page. **UC-16.0. E2 Payment Gateway Unavailable** 1\. The system detects that the user is not an authenticated Learner or Teacher. 2\. The system displays a permission error message (MSG11). 3\. The system does not create a payment transaction. 4\. The use case ends. **UC-16.0. E3 Premium Activation Failed After Successful Payment** 1\. At step 7 or step 8 of the Normal Flow, the system cannot connect to the Payment Gateway or cannot verify the payment. 2\. The system records the transaction as pending or failed according to system rules. 3\. The system displays a payment not completed message (MSG43). 4\. Premium access is not activated. **UC-16.0.E4 Premium Activation Failed After Successful Payment** 1\. At step 11 of the Normal Flow, the payment is successful, but the system fails to update the user’s Premium status due to a database or system error. 2\. The system records the successful payment transaction. 3\. The system marks the subscription for retry or manual support handling. 4\. The system does not lose the payment record. 5\. The system displays a data loading or system error message (MSG13) and informs the user that activation is being processed. **UC-16.0.E5 Payment Expired or Cannot Be Verified** 1\. At step 9 or step 10 of the Normal Flow, the Payment Gateway returns an expired or unverified payment status. 2\. The system records the transaction as expired or unverified. 3\. The system displays MSG43. 4\. Premium access is not activated. |                   |                                |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |                                |
| Frequency of Use:  | Medium. This use case occurs when Learners or Teachers decide to purchase Premium access, especially after encountering Premium-only features.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |                   |                                |
| Business Rules:    | BR-07, BR-11, BR-12, BR-15, BR-16, BR-17                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |                                |
| Other Information: | Payment logs should be retained for audit, refund support, and dispute resolution. Premium activation should depend only on a verified successful payment confirmation from the Payment Gateway.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |                                |
| Assumptions:       | The Payment Gateway can return reliable payment status responses, and the system can map each payment transaction to the correct user account and selected Premium plan.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |                                |

####

### **2.9 System Admin** {#2.9-system-admin}

#### **_2.9.1 View user list_** {#2.9.1-view-user-list}

| ID and Name:       | UC-51 View user list                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Lê Hải Đăng                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             | Date Created:     | 24/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Admin                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   | Secondary Actors: | None      |
| Description:       | As an Admin, I want to view the list of users in the system so that I can monitor user accounts and support account management.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The Admin opens the User Management page from the Admin dashboard.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Admin has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The Admin account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The active role is Admin. PRE-4. The Admin has permission to access user management.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The system displays the user list. POST-2. The Admin can search, filter, and select a user for further account status management. POST-3. No user account data is changed by viewing the list.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-51.0 View User List** 1\. The Admin opens the User Management page. 2\. The system verifies Admin authorization. 3\. The system retrieves the user account list. 4\. The system displays user summary information such as name, email, role, account status, and created date where applicable. 5\. The Admin searches or filters users by keyword, role, account status, or date range. 6\. The system displays matching users. 7\. The Admin selects a user to view more details or proceed to UC-52 Update user account status. |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-51.1 No Matching Users Found** 1\. At step 6, the system finds no users matching the search or filter condition. 2\. The system displays MSG45. 3\. The Admin may adjust the filter or clear the search condition.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-51.0.E1 Unauthorized Access** 1\. At step 2, the system detects that the user is not an Admin or lacks permission. 2\. The system blocks access and displays MSG11. **UC-51.0.E2 Failed To Load User List** 1\. At step 3, the system cannot load user data. 2\. The system displays MSG13. **UC-51.0.E3 Session Expired** 1\. At any step, the Admin session expires. 2\. The system displays MSG50 and redirects the Admin to log in again.                                                                                      |                   |           |
| Priority:          | High                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | High. Admins use this feature when reviewing or managing system users.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-11, BR-12, BR-40                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |           |
| Other Information: | The user list must not expose passwords, sensitive authentication data, payment records, or private security details.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The system supports Admin search and filtering for user management.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |                   |           |

#### **_2.9.2 Update user account status_** {#2.9.2-update-user-account-status}

| ID and Name:       | UC-52 Update user account status                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Lê Hải Đăng                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           | Date Created:     | 24/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Admin                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 | Secondary Actors: | None      |
| Description:       | As an Admin, I want to update a user account status such as active, suspended, or banned so that I can control system access according to platform rules.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The Admin selects a user from the User Management page and chooses an account status update action.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Admin has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The Admin account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The active role is Admin. PRE-4. The Admin has permission to update user account status. PRE-5. The target user account exists.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The target user account status is updated successfully. POST-2. The updated status controls the target user’s future access to protected features. POST-3. The system records the Admin action for accountability. POST-4. If the action fails or is cancelled, the target user account status remains unchanged.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-52.0 Update User Account Status** 1\. The Admin opens the User Management page. 2\. The Admin selects a target user account. 3\. The system displays the user detail and current account status. 4\. The Admin chooses a new account status such as Active, Suspended, or Banned. 5\. The system asks the Admin to confirm the account status update. 6\. The Admin confirms the update. 7\. The system validates Admin authorization and the selected status. 8\. The system updates the target user account status. 9\. The system records the Admin action in the audit log. 10\. The system displays MSG46.                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-52.1 Cancel Status Update** 1\. At step 5, the Admin cancels the confirmation. 2\. The system closes the confirmation message. 3\. The target user account status remains unchanged. **UC-52.2 Add Status Update Reason** 1\. At step 4 or step 5, the system asks the Admin to provide a reason for the status update. 2\. The Admin enters a reason. 3\. The system stores the reason with the audit log. 4\. The flow continues from step 6\.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-52.0.E1 Unauthorized Status Update** 1\. At step 7, the system detects that the Admin does not have permission to update account status. 2\. The system blocks the action and displays MSG11. **UC-52.0.E2 Invalid Account Status** 1\. At step 7, the system detects an invalid or unsupported account status. 2\. The system displays MSG03. 3\. The Admin selects a valid account status. 4\. The flow continues from step 4\. **UC-52.0.E3 Target User Not Found** 1\. At step 2 or step 7, the system cannot find the selected target user account. 2\. The system displays MSG45. 3\. The use case ends. **UC-52.0.E4 Session Expired** 1\. At any step, the Admin session expires. 2\. The system displays MSG50 and redirects the Admin to log in again. |                   |           |
| Priority:          | Medium                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | Medium. Admins use this feature to control access for problematic or restored accounts.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-11, BR-12, BR-40                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |           |
| Other Information: | This use case updates account status only. It does not grant or remove system roles.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The system defines valid account statuses such as Active, Suspended, and Banned.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |           |

#### **_2.9.3 Hide public learning resource_** {#2.9.3-hide-public-learning-resource}

| ID and Name:       | UC-53 Hide public learning resource                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| :----------------- | :------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :-------- |
| Created By:        | Lê Hải Đăng                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          | Date Created:     | 24/5/2026 |
| Primary Actor:     | Admin                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | Secondary Actors: | None      |
| Description:       | As an Admin, I want to hide inappropriate or invalid public learning resources so that users cannot access unsuitable public content.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                   |           |
| Trigger:           | The Admin selects a public learning resource and clicks Hide or Remove from Public.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Admin has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The Admin account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The active role is Admin. PRE-4. The Admin has permission to manage public learning resources. PRE-5. The selected public learning resource exists.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |           |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The selected learning resource is hidden from public access. POST-2. The resource no longer appears in public search results. POST-3. The system records the Admin action for accountability. POST-4. Historical learning records, quiz attempts, exam records, and reports related to the resource remain preserved if required by system rules.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |           |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-53.0 Hide Public Learning Resource** 1\. The Admin opens the Resource Management page. 2\. The system displays public learning resources such as public Study Sets or other public learning content. 3\. The Admin searches or selects a public learning resource to review. 4\. The system displays the selected resource detail page. 5\. The Admin clicks Hide or Remove from Public. 6\. The system displays a confirmation message. 7\. The Admin confirms the hide action. 8\. The system validates Admin authorization and resource status. 9\. The system updates the resource visibility status to hidden or inactive. 10\. The system removes the resource from public search results and public access. 11\. The system records the Admin action in the audit log. 12\. The system displays MSG47.                                                   |                   |           |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-53.1 Hide Resource From Resource List** 1\. The Admin opens the public resource list**.** 2\. The Admin clicks Hide directly on a selected resource row. 3\. The system displays a confirmation message. 4\. The Admin confirms the action. 5\. The flow continues from step 8 of the Normal Flow. **UC-53.2 Add Hide Reason** 1\. At step 6, the system asks the Admin to provide a reason for hiding the resource. 2\. The Admin enters a reason such as inappropriate content, incorrect information, duplicate content, or policy violation. 3\. The system saves the reason with the audit log. 4\. The flow continues from step 7\. **UC-53.3 Cancel Hide Action** 1\. At step 6, the Admin clicks Cancel. 2\. The system cancels the hide action. 3\. The selected resource remains public and unchanged.                                                |                   |           |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-53.0.E1 Unauthorized Hide Action** 1\. At step 8, the system detects that the user is not authorized to hide public learning resources. 2\. The system blocks the action and displays MSG11. **UC-53.0.E2 Resource Not Found** 1\. At step 3 or step 8, the system cannot find the selected learning resource. 2\. The system displays MSG45. 3\. The use case ends. **UC-53.0.E3 Resource Already Hidden** 1\. At step 8, the system detects that the selected resource has already been hidden or deactivated. 2\. The system displays the current resource status. 3\. The use case ends. **UC-53.0.E4 Hide Action Restricted** 1\. At step 8, the system detects that the selected resource cannot be hidden due to system restrictions or protected status. 2\. The system displays MSG48. 3\. The use case ends without changing the resource visibility. |                   |           |
| Priority:          | Medium                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| Frequency of Use:  | Medium. Admins use this feature when moderating public learning resources and maintaining platform content quality.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Business Rules:    | BR-02, BR-12, BR-40                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |           |
| Other Information: | Hiding a public resource should not permanently delete historical learning data, quiz attempts, exam attempts, or reports that reference the resource.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |                   |           |
| Assumptions:       | The Admin can evaluate whether a public resource should be hidden based on platform rules, content quality, or user reports.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |                   |           |

#### **_2.9.4 View system status_** {#2.9.4-view-system-status}

| ID and Name:       | UC-54 View system status                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |                   |                                                                     |
| :----------------- | :-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | :---------------- | :------------------------------------------------------------------ |
| Created By:        | Lê Hải Đăng                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       | Date Created:     | 24/5/2026                                                           |
| Primary Actor:     | Admin                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             | Secondary Actors: | Supabase Authentication, Email Service, Payment Gateway, Gemini API |
| Description:       | As an Admin, I want to view system status so that I can monitor platform stability, service availability, and operational health.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                   |                                                                     |
| Trigger:           | The Admin opens the System Status page from the Admin dashboard.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |                                                                     |
| Preconditions:     | PRE-1. The Admin has logged in successfully. PRE-2. The Admin account is active and not locked. PRE-3. The active role is Admin. PRE-4. The Admin has permission to view system status.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |                                                                     |
| Postconditions:    | POST-1. The system displays operational status information. POST-2. The Admin can identify system health, service availability, recent errors, and external service status. POST-3. No system configuration is changed by viewing system status.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |                   |                                                                     |
| Normal Flow:       | **UC-54.0 View System Status** 1\. The Admin opens the System Status page. 2\. The system verifies Admin authorization. 3\. The system retrieves platform health information. 4\. The system checks or retrieves status information for Supabase Authentication, Email Service, Payment Gateway, and Gemini API where available. 5\. The system displays system status indicators, recent errors, service availability, and operational health information. 6\. The Admin reviews the system status dashboard. 7\. The Admin refreshes the status page if needed. 8\. The system reloads the latest available status information. |                   |                                                                     |
| Alternative Flows: | **UC-54.1 Partial System Status Available** 1\. At step 4, one or more external services cannot be checked. 2\. The system displays available status data. 3\. The system displays MSG49 for unavailable service status information. **UC-54.2 No Critical Issue Found** 1\. At step 5, the system detects that all monitored services are operating normally. 2\. The system displays normal operational status indicators. 3\. The Admin continues monitoring or exits the page.                                                                                                                                                |                   |                                                                     |
| Exceptions:        | **UC-54.0.E1 Unauthorized Status Access** 1\. At step 2, the system detects that the user is not an Admin or lacks permission. 2\. The system blocks access and displays MSG11. **UC-54.0.E2 Failed To Load System Status** 1\. At step 3, the system cannot load system status information. 3\. The system displays MSG13. **UC-54.0.E3 Session Expired** 1\. At any step, the Admin session expires. 2\. The system displays MSG50 and redirects the Admin to log in again.                                                                                                                                                     |                   |                                                                     |
| Priority:          | Medium                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                   |                                                                     |
| Frequency of Use:  | Medium. Admins use this feature to monitor platform stability and service availability.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                   |                                                                     |
| Business Rules:    | BR-12, BR-40                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                   |                                                                     |
| Other Information: | This use case is for monitoring only. It does not include changing system configuration or restarting services.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |                                                                     |
| Assumptions:       | The system can retrieve platform health information and available external service status data.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |                   |                                                                     |

#### **_3.1.1 View Landing Page_** {#3.1.1-view-landing-page}

![][image15]![][image16]![][image17]![][image18]

This screen allows the Guest to:

- view public study entry points, search public sets, preview study modes, and navigate to account entry screens.

- use the visible fields and actions listed in the Field Description table.

On the screen, s/he can also:

- view status, validation, empty, pagination, or mock interaction states where applicable.

| Field Name          | Description                               |
| :------------------ | :---------------------------------------- |
| Hero Search Keyword | Search public study sets and users        |
| Hero Search Action  | Button to search when entered keyword     |
| Study Mode Cards    | Display short information for study modes |
| Open Flashcards     | Button to open flashcards                 |

- use the visible fields and actions listed in the Field Description table.

On the screen, s/he can also:

- view status, validation, empty, pagination, or mock interaction states where applicable.

| Field Name                    | Description                                                          |
| :---------------------------- | :------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Keyword                       | Text search field. User enters keyword(s) to filter visible records. |
| Study Mode                    | Filter study sets by study mode                                      |
| Rating Filter                 | Filter study sets by rating                                          |
| Sort By                       | Sort study sets by selected criteria                                 |
| Apply                         | Button to execute search and apply filters                           |
| Advanced                      | Button to toggle advanced filter options                             |
| Reset Filters                 | Button to clear all search inputs and filters                        |
| Public Study Set Result Cards | List displaying searched public study sets                           |
| Open Sample Set               | Button to open a sample study set                                    |
| View Detail                   | Button to view detailed information of a study set                   |
| Pagination                    | Navigate between pages of search results                             |

### **3.2 Authentication & Profile** {#3.2-authentication-&-profile}

#### **_3.2.1 Register Account_** {#3.2.1-register-account}

![][image21]

This screen allows the user to:

· create a learner or teacher account with role request, learning goal, credential fields, and validation feedback.

· use Google sign-up mock or navigate to login.

On the screen, s/he can also:

· view validation messages after submitting incomplete or invalid data.

Field Description

| Field Name           | Description                                                                                |
| :------------------- | :----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Full Name            | Text input. User enters display name.                                                      |
| Email Address        | Email input. Required account email.                                                       |
| Phone Number         | Text input. User enters contact phone number.                                              |
| Username             | Text input. User enters username.                                                          |
| Requested Role       | Dropdown/select field. User chooses Learner or Teacher.                                    |
| Password             | Password field. User enters new account password.                                          |
| Confirm Password     | Password field. Must match Password.                                                       |
| Learning Goal        | Dropdown/select field. User chooses main learning goal.                                    |
| Referral Code        | Text input. Optional invitation or referral code.                                          |
| Create Account       | Action field. Submits registration form.                                                   |
| Continue With Google | Action field. Starts Google sign-up mock.                                                  |
| Already Have Account | Action field. Opens Login screen.                                                          |
| Validation Message   | Visible message/state field. Shows required-field, email, password, or confirmation error. |

####

####

####

####

####

####

#### **_3.2.2 Login With Account And Google Login_** {#3.2.2-login-with-account-and-google-login}

![][image22]

This screen allows the user to:

· login using email or username and password.

· use Google login mock, recover password, create account, or logout current user.

On the screen, s/he can also:

· toggle password visibility and choose remember-login preference.

Field Description

| Field Name        | Description                                                                        |
| :---------------- | :--------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Register Tab      | Action field. Opens Register Account screen.                                       |
| Login Tab         | Visible tab field. Shows current login tab.                                        |
| Login With Google | Action field. Starts Google login mock.                                            |
| Email             | Email/text input. User enters email or username.                                   |
| Password          | Password field. User enters password.                                              |
| Show Password     | Action field. Toggles password visibility.                                         |
| Remember Me       | Checkbox field. User chooses persistent login preference.                          |
| Forgot Password   | Action field. Opens Forgot Password screen.                                        |
| Login             | Action field. Submits login form.                                                  |
| Create Account    | Action field. Opens Register Account screen.                                       |
| Logout            | Action field. Signs out current signed-in account when visible.                    |
| Status Message    | Visible message/state field. Shows required-field, logout, or Google mock message. |

#### **_3.2.3 Forgot Password_** {#3.2.3-forgot-password}

![][image23]

This screen allows the user to:

· enter registered email and choose delivery method before any verification code is entered.

· send verification code, enter the received code, verify the code, then continue to Reset Password.

On the screen, s/he can also:

· return to login before verification or continue to reset password after code verification succeeds.

Field Description

| Field Name               | Description                                                                      |
| :----------------------- | :------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Registered Email Address | Email input. User enters account email to receive verification code.             |
| Reset Delivery Method    | Dropdown/select field. User chooses Email code or SMS code.                      |
| Account Username         | Text input. Optional username for account verification.                          |
| Verification Code        | Text input. Disabled until code is sent; user enters received verification code. |
| Send Verification Code   | Action field. Sends verification code in production.                             |
| Verify Code              | Action field. Checks whether entered verification code is valid.                 |
| Back To Login            | Action field. Returns to Login screen before code verification.                  |
| Continue Reset Password  | Action field. Opens Reset Password screen after verification succeeds.           |
| Code Sent Message        | Visible message/state field. Shows code delivery status.                         |
| Code Verified Message    | Visible message/state field. Shows accepted verification code status.            |

#### **_3.2.4 Reset Password_** {#3.2.4-reset-password}

![][image24]

This screen allows the user to:

· reset password from the signed-in profile security area.

· request a verification token for the current account email, then enter new password and confirmation.

On the screen, s/he can also:

· return to profile edit and view token-sent or reset-success messages.

Field Description

| Field Name              | Description                                                                        |
| :---------------------- | :--------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Account Email           | Read-only field. Shows current signed-in account email; user does not re-enter it. |
| Verification Token      | Text input. User enters token received by email.                                   |
| Send Verification Token | Action field. Sends token to current account email in production.                  |
| New Password            | Password field. User enters new password.                                          |
| Confirm New Password    | Password field. Must match New Password.                                           |
| Logout Other Devices    | Dropdown/select field. User chooses whether to invalidate other sessions.          |
| Reset Password          | Action field. Submits password reset for current account.                          |
| Back To Profile Edit    | Action field. Returns to Edit Personal Profile screen.                             |

| Notification Preference  | View-only data field. Shows notification preference.                            |

#### **_3.2.6 Edit Personal Profile_** {#3.2.6-edit-personal-profile}

![][image26]

This screen allows the user to:

· update allowed profile fields, notification settings, visibility, and profile details.

· open Reset Password from profile editing area.

On the screen, s/he can also:

· save changes, cancel, or view saved confirmation.

Field Description

| Field Name              | Description                                                            |
| :---------------------- | :--------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Reset Password          | Action field. Opens profile security Reset Password screen.            |
| Full Name               | Text input. User edits display name.                                   |
| Phone Number            | Text input. User edits contact phone number.                           |
| Avatar Initials         | Text input. Maximum 2 characters for avatar display.                   |
| Username                | Text input. User edits username.                                       |
| Preferred Language      | Text input. User edits language preference.                            |
| Timezone                | Text input. User edits timezone.                                       |
| Notification Preference | Dropdown/select field. User chooses Email, In-app, or Email \+ in-app. |
| Profile Visibility      | Dropdown/select field. User chooses public or private profile.         |
| Change role             | Action field. Change role to teacher/student.                          |
| Profile Details         | Textarea field. User edits profile bio/details.                        |
| Save Changes            | Action field. Saves profile updates.                                   |
| Cancel                  | Action field. Returns to profile screen without saving.                |
| Saved Message           | Visible message/state field. Shows save confirmation.                  |
