#### **_3.2.8 Notification Center_** {#3.2.8-notification-center}

![][image28]

This screen allows the user to:

· view notifications, search and filter them, mark notifications as read, and clear read items.

· Use the visible fields and actions listed in the Field Description table.

On the screen, s/he can also:

· View status, validation, empty, pagination, or mock interaction states where applicable.

Field Description

| Field Name               | Description                                                                                  |
| :----------------------- | :------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Search Notifications     | Text search field. User enters keyword(s) to filter visible records.                         |
| Read Status              | Status field. User views or selects status depending on the screen context.                  |
| Notification Type        | Visible field. User views or enters this value on the screen.                                |
| Sort By                  | Dropdown/select field. User chooses one visible option to configure or filter the screen.    |
| Apply                    | Action field. User clicks to navigate, submit, update, or process the selected visible item. |
| Reset Filters            | Action field. User clicks to navigate, submit, update, or process the selected visible item. |
| Mark All As Read         | Action field. User clicks to navigate, submit, update, or process the selected visible item. |
| Clear Read Notifications | Visible field. User views or enters this value on the screen.                                |
| Notification List        | Visible data group. Shows records or grouped screen data. Counted as one field.              |

| Pagination               | Action field. User clicks to navigate, submit, update, or process the selected visible item. |

| Field Name             | Description                                                                                 |

| Class                  | Read-only text; displays the name of the class associated with the exam                     |
| Start Time             | Read-only text; displays the scheduled start date and time of the exam                      |
| Duration               | Read-only text; displays the total allowed time to complete the exam                        |
| Attempts Allowed       | Read-only text; displays the maximum number of attempts granted to the user                 |
| Result Visibility      | Read-only text; indicates when the final exam results will be revealed                      |
| Randomization          | Read-only text; specifies the randomization rules applied to the exam questions and answers |

| Passing Score               | Numeric input field; sets the minimum score required to pass                                      |
| Exam Access Code            | Text input field; configures a specific code required for learners to join the exam               |
| Late Join Grace Period      | Text/numeric input field; defines the allowed buffer time for latecomers                          |
| Auto-submit Before End      | Text/numeric input field; configures the automatic submission countdown before the deadline       |
| Number of Questions         | Numeric input field; specifies the exact number of questions to be drawn from the selected source |
| Result Visibility           | Dropdown menu; configures whether learners see completion only, score only, or question-answer review |
| Review Permission           | Dropdown menu; defines what parts of the exam learners can review                                 |
| Exam Password               | Secure text input field; optionally sets a password to restrict exam access                       |
| Candidate Instructions      | Text input field; provides specific rules or guidelines for learners before starting              |
| Randomize Questions         | Checkbox; toggles the shuffling of question order for each learner                                |
| Randomize Answers           | Checkbox; toggles the shuffling of answer options for each question                               |
| Enable Auto-save            | Checkbox; toggles automatic saving of exam progress                                               |
| Require Full-screen Warning | Checkbox; toggles alerts if the learner attempts to exit full-screen mode                         |
| Lock Navigation After Start | Checkbox; restricts learners from navigating away from the exam window                            |
| Notify Learners Before Exam | Checkbox; toggles sending an automated notification to learners before the exam starts            |
| Create Exam Session         | Primary action button; submits the form to create the new exam session                            |

· view learner progress metrics, filter by subject and period, and review weak subjects.

## **4\. Non-Functional Requirements** {#4.-non-functional-requirements}

### **4.1 External Interfaces** {#4.1-external-interfaces}

This section outlines how the platform interacts with human users, hardware components, and external software services.

**1\. User Interfaces (UI):** The system must provide a clean, modern web-based user interface accessible via desktop, tablet, and mobile browsers. The interface design must feature intuitive layout flows, meaning primary actions (such as launching Study flashcards or viewing Joined classes) are accessible within a maximum of three clicks from the user dashboard.

**2\. Hardware Interfaces:** The platform has no dedicated hardware interface requirements. It runs entirely within standard web browsers on client devices (Personal Computers, Laptops, Smartphones). The system must run smoothly on low-to-mid-tier client devices without causing CPU spikes or thermal throttling.

**3\. Software Interfaces:**

- **Authentication Engine:** The platform interfaces with Supabase Authentication via secure HTTPS API integrations to process user registration, identity handshakes (Log in with Google), and password updates.

- **AI Services Layer:** The backend communicates with the external Google Gemini API over secure REST endpoints to handle dynamic query pipelines, request AI answer explanations, and handle programmatic study question generation.

- **Payment Gateway Interface:** The system integrates with a third-party payment infrastructure ecosystem (e.g., VNPAY or Stripe) to offload secure cardholder data handling and track invoice payment approvals during plan updates (Upgrade to Premium).

- **Data Tier:** The application communicates with a relational data layer via standard JDBC/ODBC connection pooling protocols to execute transactional read/write events.

### **4.2 Quality Attributes** {#4.2-quality-attributes}

#### **4.2.1 Usability** {#4.2.1-usability}

- **Onboarding & Training Time:** The platform must be designed for zero-training execution. A standard user (Learner or Teacher) should be capable of successfully operating primary features—like navigating classes or reviewing study dashboards—within 5 to 10 minutes of exposure without reading documentation.
- **UI Standards Compliance:** The user interface layouts must follow modern mobile-responsive layout practices. The text elements, status markers, and graphics must maintain standard accessibility color contrast thresholds (minimum 4.5:1 ratio conforming to WCAG 2.1 Level AA standards) so all learner populations can view learning materials under variable lighting environments.

#### **4.2.2 Performance** {#4.2.2-performance}

- **Transaction & Page Response Times:**
  - Normal Conditions: Under standard user traffic weights (defined as 100 concurrent active users or less), 95% of all standard page transactions and dashboard loads must complete in 3.0 seconds or less.
  - Stress Conditions: Under peak stress loads (defined as more than 100 concurrent active users, scaling up to an upper baseline of 500 users), the platform must guarantee execution stability, with 90% of all page loads or processing pipelines completing within 10.0 seconds or less.
- **Throughput & Capacity Limitations:**
  - The application architecture must comfortably sustain a baseline capacity of up to 100 concurrent active browser sessions without suffering service crashes.
  - The system database must be optimized using indices to handle up to 50 transactional write commitments per second during high-intensity exam periods.
- **Resource Utilization Metrics:**
  - Client-Side Memory: The frontend web page instance running inside a client browser application must keep its memory allocation footprint under 300MB during active testing or flashcard operations.
  - Server-Side Bandwidth: Data transmission payloads for core analytical data views (View learning analytics) must utilize JSON data optimization to ensure file transfer sizes remain lightweight. Large batch operations, like document data serialization loops (Export report), must be handled asynchronously.

#### **_4.2.3 Security_** {#4.2.3-security}

- **Role-Based Access Control (RBAC):** The system must strictly enforce role privileges. Users authenticated with a "Learner" role must be completely blocked from accessing backend API endpoints or UI views reserved for "Teacher" or "Admin" roles, returning an HTTP 403 Forbidden status code.
- **Data Encryption & Transport:** All data transmitted between the client browser and the system backend, as well as communications with Supabase Authentication and the Google Gemini API, must be encrypted in transit using TLS 1.3 (HTTPS). Sensitive data at rest, including user profile properties (phone numbers, email hashes) and official exam grade logs, must be encrypted using AES-256 standards.
- **Token Lifecycle Security:** Session authentication must rely on stateless JSON Web Tokens (JWT) managed securely. Access tokens must have a brief validity window (e.g., 1 hour), requiring secure Refresh Tokens to request updates silently. Upon executing the Log out account, client-side token storage must be entirely cleared, and the server must invalidate the active refresh token.
- **Input Sanitization:** To safeguard the application against SQL Injection and Cross-Site Scripting (XSS) threats, all user-submitted text data—specifically questions authored by teachers or bulk roster spreadsheets uploaded via Excel—must be scrubbed and sanitized at the API layer before database commit actions occur.

#### **4.2.4 Availability** {#4.2.4-availability}

- **System Uptime Baseline:** The platform must maintain an operational availability SLA of 99.5% or higher over any calendar month.
- **Scheduled Maintenance Windows:** Anticipated system upgrades, database migrations, or server reboots must be restricted to off-peak usage windows (specifically between 2:00 AM and 4:00 AM GMT+7) and must be announced to users at least 24 hours in advance.
- **Exam Session Fault Tolerance:** During active testing execution (Take exam), the system must execute an automated asynchronous background save of the learner's selected answers every 30 seconds. If the learner suffers an abrupt local network drop or a browser crash, they must be allowed to log back in and resume the exam seamlessly without losing any previously recorded progress.
- **Graceful Degradation:** If an external dependent dependency experiences an outage (e.g., the Google Gemini API rate limits or drops offline), the primary ecosystem must continue running normally. The system must display a temporary error notice for AI features (like requesting answer explanations) while ensuring core non-AI functionalities (taking quizzes, viewing classes, downloading reports) remain fully accessible.

#### **4.2.5 Compatibility** {#4.2.5-compatibility}

- **Cross-Browser Operations:** The user interface layout and client script execution must behave consistently and flawlessly across the latest stable production releases of all primary modern browsers, including Google Chrome, Apple Safari, Mozilla Firefox, and Microsoft Edge.
- **Responsive Layout Breakpoints:** The application viewport rendering must adapt smoothly across variable form factors:
  - **Mobile Optimization:** Core learner features, such as studying flashcards or checking profiles, must scale perfectly down to mobile screens (360px to 480px width layouts).
  - **Desktop Optimization:** Data-dense management interfaces, such as the teacher's analytical reporting view, must be structurally optimized for desktop aspect ratios (1024px width and above).
- **Data File Standards Compatibility:** The bulk question template parser must remain backward-compatible, successfully handling both legacy binary spreadsheet structures and open XML spreadsheet schemas generated via Microsoft Excel, Google Sheets, or LibreOffice Calc.

#### **4.2.6 Scalability** {#4.2.6-scalability}

- **Horizontal Server Scaling:** The application backend architecture must be entirely decoupled and stateless, enabling horizontal auto-scaling (adding additional container instances behind a reverse proxy/load balancer) to distribute processing stress evenly as simultaneous traffic increases from 100 to 500 concurrent sessions.
- **Data Volume Scalability:** Database tables, specifically tables recording learner answers and public study sets, must be heavily indexed. Search query lookups must maintain an execution turnaround time of under 1.5 seconds, even as the global database grows to hold over 500,000 unique records.
- **Storage Elasticity:** The media asset repository hosting uploaded user avatars or attached lesson files must use elastic file allocation logic, ensuring that total storage bounds expand automatically without human intervention or localized server disk space depletion.

## **5\. Requirement Appendix** {#5.-requirement-appendix}

### **5.1 Business Rules** {#5.1-business-rules}

| ID    | Feature                                        | Business Rule                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| :---- | :--------------------------------------------- | :------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| BR-01 | Public Access & Discovery                      | Guests may access only public features, including viewing the landing page, searching public study sets, searching public user accounts, viewing public study set details, studying public flashcards, and viewing Premium plans.                                                                                                                                                      |
| BR-02 |                                                | Public learning resources are visible only when they are marked as Public and are not hidden, archived, deleted, restricted, or disabled by Admin.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| BR-03 |                                                | Public search and public detail pages must expose only safe public information. Private learning resources, restricted resources, sensitive account data, payment data, security data, and internal permission data must not be displayed.                                                                                                                                             |
| BR-04 |                                                | Guests may study public flashcards, but Guests must not take study set quizzes, review wrong answers, view personal learning progress, join classes, take exams, request AI answer explanations, create content, or access role-specific dashboards.                                                                                                                                   |
| BR-05 | Authentication & Account Security              | Each user account must be associated with one unique email address. The system must reject registration if the submitted email already belongs to an existing account.                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| BR-06 |                                                | Password-related actions must satisfy the platform password policy. The confirmation password must match the new password before registration, password reset, or password change is accepted.                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| BR-07 |                                                | The system must manage authentication sessions securely. Users must log in before accessing protected features, and logout must invalidate the current session.                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| BR-08 |                                                | After a configurable number of consecutive failed login attempts, the account must be temporarily locked or protected according to the account security policy.                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| BR-09 |                                                | Google login must authenticate the user through the external authentication provider. If the Google email matches an existing platform account, the system must retrieve or link the corresponding account instead of creating a duplicate account.                                                                                                                                    |
| BR-10 |                                                | Password reset links or tokens must be time-limited, single-use, and invalidated immediately after successful password reset.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| BR-11 | Account Status Control                         | Locked, suspended, banned, deleted, or inactive accounts must not access protected system features until the account status is restored by an authorized process.                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| BR-12 | Authorization & Role Management                | The system must enforce Role-Based Access Control. Each protected feature must be accessible only by the actor roles defined in the official use case list.                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| BR-13 |                                                | Learner and Teacher users may switch their active role between Learner and Teacher. Admin access must not be granted through role switching.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| BR-14 | Profile Management                             | Users may view and update only their own allowed profile and password information. Protected fields such as account status, system permissions, payment records, and Admin privileges must not be directly modified by normal users.                                                                                                                                                   |
| BR-15 | Payment & Subscription                         | Guests, Learners, and Teachers may view Premium plans and benefits, but only authenticated Learners and Teachers may upgrade to Premium.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| BR-16 |                                                | Premium access must be activated only after the Payment Gateway confirms a successful transaction. Failed, cancelled, expired, or unverified payments must not activate Premium access.                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| BR-17 |                                                | Premium-only features must be available only to users with active Premium access. Expired or inactive Premium accounts must be treated as non-Premium accounts.                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| BR-18 | Class Management                               | Teachers may create and manage only classes they own or are assigned to manage. Learners and Guests must not perform Teacher class management actions.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| BR-19 |                                                | Learners may join a class only through a valid, active, and non-expired class code or invitation link.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| BR-20 |                                                | A Learner cannot join the same class more than once. Duplicate class memberships and duplicate pending join requests must be rejected by the system.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| BR-21 |                                                | If a class requires Teacher approval, the Learner must not become an official class member until the Teacher approves the join request.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| BR-22 |                                                | Removing a Learner from a class must revoke future access to class-only study sets, exams, and activities, while preserving historical learning records, exam attempts, and reports.                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| BR-23 | Study Set Management & Learning Study Set      | Users may access study sets only according to visibility, ownership, class assignment, and authorization rules.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| BR-24 |                                                | Teachers may create study sets and assign study sets only to classes they manage. A study set must contain required metadata before it can be saved or assigned.                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| BR-25 |                                                | Flashcard study is available to Guests only for public study sets and to authenticated users only for study sets they are allowed to access.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| BR-26 |                                                | Only authenticated Learners may take study set quizzes, review their own wrong answers, and have their learning progress recorded.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| BR-27 | Analytics & Learning Progress                  | Learners may view only their own quiz history, wrong answers, learning progress, accuracy rate, repeated mistakes, and weak subjects.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| BR-28 | Question Bank Repository                       | Question Banks are Teacher-managed repositories. Teachers may view, create, update, delete, archive, or hide only Question Banks they own or are authorized to manage.                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| BR-29 |                                                | Each Question Bank must have required repository information such as title, description, subject, visibility, owner, or repository configuration before it can be saved or updated.                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| BR-30 |                                                | A Question Bank that is referenced by study sets, exam sessions, reports, or historical records must not be permanently deleted if deletion would break data integrity. The system must archive, hide, deactivate, or prevent deletion instead.                                                                                                                                        |
| BR-31 | Question Management                            | Teachers may add, import, preview, update, or delete questions only inside owned or authorized Study Sets and Question Banks.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| BR-32 |                                                | A question cannot be saved unless it has valid question content, supported question type, answer data, correct answer, and required scoring information.                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| BR-33 |                                                | Imported Excel files must follow the required system template. Invalid rows must not be saved and must be reported with row-level validation errors before valid questions are saved.                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| BR-34 |                                                | Manually entered, imported, copied, or AI-generated questions must be previewed before they are saved into an authorized Study Set or Question Bank.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| BR-35 |                                                | Questions used in active exams, completed attempts, learning records, or reports must not be modified or deleted in a way that corrupts historical data. The system must use versioning, archiving, hiding, or update restriction when needed.                                                                                                                                         |
| BR-36 | AI Features                                    | AI answer explanation and AI question generation are Premium-only features. AI-generated content may be used only within the user’s authorized learning or question management scope.                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| BR-37 |                                                | If Gemini API is unavailable, rate-limited, or returns an error, the system must display an appropriate message and allow non-AI core features to continue where possible.                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| BR-38 | Exam Session Management                        | Only Teachers may create, configure, and view official exam sessions for classes they manage. Learners may access and take only published exams assigned to classes they have joined.                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| BR-39 |                                                | An exam session may be published only when it has a managed class, valid selected questions or authorized Question Banks, valid time settings, valid attempt limit, and result visibility configuration.                                                                                                                                                                               |
| BR-40 | Exam Result, Analytics & System Administration | Exam attempts must be locked after submission or auto-submission, and exam result visibility must follow the Teacher's configuration: completion only, score only, or question-answer review. Teachers may view and export analytics only within their authorized scope. Admins may manage user account status, hide invalid public learning resources, view system status, and significant Admin actions must be recorded for accountability. |

###

### **5.2 System Messages** {#5.2-system-messages}

| ID    | Message Type | Context                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      | Content                                                                                                                                      |
| ----- | ------------ | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| MSG01 | Success      | User registers an account successfully.                                                                                                                                                                                                      | Your account has been created successfully.                                                                                                  |
| MSG02 | Error        | User leaves required information empty, such as email, password, study set name, question bank name, class information, question data, or exam configuration.                                                                                | Please complete all required information.                                                                                                    |
| MSG03 | Error        | User enters invalid data, such as mismatched password confirmation, invalid input format, invalid class code, expired token, invalid Excel file format, or invalid exam setting.                                                             | The information is invalid. Please check and try again.                                                                                      |
| MSG04 | Error        | Registration email already exists in the system.                                                                                                                                                                                             | This email is already associated with another account.                                                                                       |
| MSG05 | Error        | User enters incorrect email or password during login.                                                                                                                                                                                        | Incorrect email or password. Please try again.                                                                                               |
| MSG06 | Notification | Account is temporarily locked after multiple failed login attempts.                                                                                                                                                                          | Your account has been temporarily locked. Please try again later or reset your password.                                                     |
| MSG07 | Success      | User logs in successfully.                                                                                                                                                                                                                   | Login successful. Welcome back.                                                                                                              |
| MSG08 | Success      | User logs out successfully.                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | You have been logged out successfully.                                                                                                       |
| MSG09 | Notification | System sends password reset email successfully.                                                                                                                                                                                              | A password reset link has been sent to your email.                                                                                           |
| MSG10 | Success      | User updates personal profile successfully.                                                                                                                                                                                                  | Your profile has been updated successfully.                                                                                                  |
| MSG11 | Error        | User accesses a feature or resource without permission, such as Guest accessing protected features, Learner accessing Teacher functions, Teacher accessing unauthorized resources, or Admin-only features being accessed by non-Admin users. | You do not have permission to access or perform this action.                                                                                 |
| MSG12 | Success      | User completes a flashcard study session.                                                                                                                                                                                                    | Flashcard study session completed.                                                                                                           |
| MSG13 | Error        | System cannot load public content, flashcards, quiz, study set, question bank, class, exam, analytics, report, or system status data due to network or system error.                                                                         | Failed to load data. Please check your connection and try again.                                                                             |
| MSG14 | Success      | Learner completes a study set quiz.                                                                                                                                                                                                          | Quiz completed. Your score and progress have been saved.                                                                                     |
| MSG15 | Notification | Learner has no wrong answers to review.                                                                                                                                                                                                      | You do not have any wrong answers to review.                                                                                                 |
| MSG16 | Error        | User does not have active Premium access but requests a Premium-only feature.                                                                                                                                                                | This feature is available for Premium accounts only. Please upgrade to continue.                                                             |
| MSG17 | Processing   | System is sending a request to Gemini API to generate an answer explanation or questions from material.                                                                                                                                      | The system is processing your AI request. Please wait.                                                                                       |
| MSG18 | Error        | Gemini API fails, times out, is rate-limited, or returns no usable content.                                                                                                                                                                  | AI processing is currently unavailable. Please try again later.                                                                              |
| MSG19 | Success      | Learner sends a class join request successfully.                                                                                                                                                                                             | Your class join request has been sent successfully.                                                                                          |
| MSG20 | Notification | Learner attempts to join a class they already belong to or has already requested to join.                                                                                                                                                    | You are already a member of this class or already have a pending join request.                                                               |
| MSG21 | Success      | Teacher creates a class successfully.                                                                                                                                                                                                        | Class created successfully. A class code or invitation link has been generated.                                                              |
| MSG22 | Success      | Teacher approves a learner’s class join request.                                                                                                                                                                                             | The learner has been approved and added to the class.                                                                                        |
| MSG23 | Success      | Teacher removes a learner from a class successfully.                                                                                                                                                                                         | The learner has been removed from the class.                                                                                                 |
| MSG24 | Error        | Learner enters an invalid, inactive, expired, or unavailable class code or invitation link.                                                                                                                                                  | The class code or invitation link is invalid, expired, or no longer available.                                                               |
| MSG25 | Success      | Teacher creates or updates a question bank successfully.                                                                                                                                                                                     | Question bank information has been saved successfully.                                                                                       |
| MSG26 | Error        | Teacher attempts to delete a question bank that is referenced by study sets, exam sessions, reports, or historical records.                                                                                                                  | This question bank cannot be permanently deleted because it is linked to existing records. You may archive or hide it instead.               |
| MSG27 | Error        | Imported Excel file contains row-level validation errors.                                                                                                                                                                                    | Some rows contain errors. Please review the error details before saving.                                                                     |
| MSG28 | Success      | Valid imported questions are saved successfully.                                                                                                                                                                                             | Questions have been imported successfully.                                                                                                   |
| MSG29 | Success      | Teacher manually adds, updates, or saves a question successfully.                                                                                                                                                                            | Question saved successfully.                                                                                                                 |
| MSG30 | Error        | Teacher attempts to update or delete a question in a way that may corrupt active exams, completed attempts, learning records, or reports.                                                                                                    | This question cannot be changed or deleted because it is linked to existing records. You may archive, hide, or create a new version instead. |
| MSG31 | Notification | Teacher must preview questions before saving.                                                                                                                                                                                                | Please preview the questions before saving them.                                                                                             |
| MSG32 | Success      | Teacher creates or updates a study set successfully.                                                                                                                                                                                         | Study set saved successfully.                                                                                                                |
| MSG33 | Success      | Teacher assigns a study set to a class successfully.                                                                                                                                                                                         | Study set assigned to class successfully.                                                                                                    |
| MSG34 | Error        | User tries to access a study set that is private, hidden, archived, deleted, restricted, or not assigned to them.                                                                                                                            | This study set is not available to you.                                                                                                      |
| MSG35 | Success      | Teacher creates an exam session successfully.                                                                                                                                                                                                | Exam session created successfully.                                                                                                           |
| MSG36 | Success      | Teacher updates exam settings successfully.                                                                                                                                                                                                  | Exam settings have been updated successfully.                                                                                                |
| MSG37 | Error        | Teacher attempts to publish an exam session with invalid settings, missing class, insufficient questions, invalid question bank, invalid time window, or missing result visibility rule.                                                     | The exam session cannot be published. Please complete the required configuration.                                                            |
| MSG38 | Error        | Learner attempts to access or take an exam that is unavailable, unpublished, outside the access period, not assigned to their class, or exceeds the allowed attempt limit.                                                                   | This exam is not available to you at this time.                                                                                              |
| MSG39 | Success      | Learner submits an exam successfully.                                                                                                                                                                                                        | Exam submitted successfully.                                                                                                                 |
| MSG40 | Notification | System auto-submits an exam when the timer expires.                                                                                                                                                                                          | Time is up. Your latest saved answers have been submitted automatically.                                                                     |
| MSG41 | Notification | Learner attempts to view an exam result that is hidden by Teacher configuration.                                                                                                                                                             | Your result is not available yet. Please check again when the teacher allows result visibility.                                              |
| MSG42 | Success      | Payment Gateway confirms successful payment and system activates Premium access.                                                                                                                                                             | Payment successful. Your Premium access has been activated.                                                                                  |
| MSG43 | Error        | Payment fails, is cancelled, expires, or cannot be verified.                                                                                                                                                                                 | Payment was not completed. Please try again or choose another payment method.                                                                |
| MSG44 | Success      | Teacher exports analytics or report successfully.                                                                                                                                                                                            | Report exported successfully.                                                                                                                |
| MSG45 | Notification | No analytics, report, search result, class member, exam, study set, question bank, or user record matches the current filter or search condition.                                                                                            | No matching data was found.                                                                                                                  |
| MSG46 | Success      | Admin updates a user account status successfully.                                                                                                                                                                                            | User account status has been updated successfully.                                                                                           |
| MSG47 | Success      | Admin hides a public learning resource successfully.                                                                                                                                                                                         | The public learning resource has been hidden successfully.                                                                                   |
| MSG48 | Error        | Admin attempts to hide a protected resource or a resource that cannot be hidden due to system restrictions.                                                                                                                                  | This resource cannot be hidden because it is protected or restricted by system rules.                                                        |
| MSG49 | Warning      | System monitoring data is partially unavailable or one or more external services cannot be checked.                                                                                                                                          | Some system status information is currently unavailable. Please refresh or check again later.                                                |
| MSG50 | Notification | User session expires while using protected features.                                                                                                                                                                                         | Your session has expired. Please log in again to continue.                                                                                   |

###

###

###

### **5.3 Security Requirements** {#5.3-security-requirements}

| ID     | Category               | Requirement                                                                                                                                      |
| ------ | ---------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ |
| SEC-01 | Authentication         | All registered users must authenticate through Supabase Authentication before accessing role-specific features.                                  |
| SEC-02 | Authorization          | The system must enforce Role-Based Access Control. Access to features must be restricted based on the assigned role: Learner, Teacher, or Admin. |
| SEC-03 | Account Protection     | User passwords and reset tokens must be securely managed. Plain text passwords must not be stored in the system database.                        |
| SEC-04 | Premium Access Control | The system must allow Premium features, such as AI explanations and AI question generation, only for users with valid Premium access.            |

### **5.4 Usability Requirements** {#5.4-usability-requirements}

| ID     | Category       | Requirement                                                                                                                                                     |
| ------ | -------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| USE-01 | UI Consistency | UI elements such as buttons, forms, modals, icons, and messages must be consistent in style and behavior across all pages.                                      |
| USE-02 | Navigation     | Users must be able to access primary features, such as Study Sets, Classes, Question Banks, Exams, Profile, and Reports, from the main navigation area.         |
| USE-03 | Error Guidance | The system must display understandable validation or error messages when users enter invalid data, access unavailable content, or perform unauthorized actions. |

###

### **5.5 Data Integrity Requirements** {#5.5-data-integrity-requirements}

| ID    | Category                | Requirement                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| ----- | ----------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| DI-01 | Input Validation        | All user-submitted data must be validated on both frontend and backend, including email, password, class code, question format, answer options, and exam settings.                                                    |
| DI-02 | Unique Constraints      | The system must prevent duplicate critical records, including duplicate active email accounts and duplicate learner membership in the same class.                                                                     |
| DI-03 | Transactional Integrity | Critical multi-step operations, such as creating an exam session, submitting an exam attempt, importing questions, or activating Premium access, must be handled consistently so partial updates do not corrupt data. |
| DI-04 | Relationship Integrity  | The system must maintain valid relationships between users, roles, classes, study sets, question banks, questions, exams, attempts, answers, payments, and reports.                                                   |

###

### **5.6 Maintainability Requirements** {#5.6-maintainability-requirements}

| ID     | Category           | Requirement                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| ------ | ------------------ | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ |
| MAI-01 | Coding Standards   | Source code must adhere to established coding conventions and naming standards for the respective language/framework.                                                                                  |
| MAI-02 | API Documentation  | All public API endpoints provided by the backend must be documented using Swagger/OpenAPI, detailing the request/response models, parameters, and status codes.                                        |
| MAI-03 | Configurable Rules | Important rules such as session timeout, failed login limit, exam duration, attempt limit, result visibility, and Premium access must be configurable instead of hard-coded.                           |
| MAI-04 | Error Logging      | The system must log important errors, including authentication failures, payment failures, AI generation failures, import failures, and exam submission failures, for troubleshooting and maintenance. |
